### [1] [ESAA-Conversational: An Event-Sourced Memory Layer for Continuity, Handoff, and Curation Across Heterogeneous LLM Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23752v1)
*Elzo Brito dos Santos Filho*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ESAA-Conversational方法，通过事件溯源实现跨多个LLM编码代理的共享对话记忆，避免状态漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多个LLM编码代理切换时，私有日志导致对话状态漂移，目标、决策等不可靠传递。

Method: 将可见对话视为事件存储，使用钩子捕获回合，规范化到activity.jsonl，投影出多个读取模型，无需LLM推理，通过命令记录持久决策。

Result: 实现了PowerShell CLI，包含多个命令，自引用案例研究显示异构代理可通过共享日志协作，无需直接通道，且保护隐私。

Conclusion: 该方法有效实现异构代理间共享对话记忆，避免状态漂移，保护隐私。

中文摘要：软件开发人员越来越多地使用多个LLM编码代理，在Codex、Grok、Claude Code等工具之间切换，当上下文窗口填满、会话结束或某个代理更适合子任务时。然而，每个代理将其对话保存在私有的、特定于供应商的日志中。结果是对话状态漂移：与一个代理建立的目标、决策、开放任务和理由在另一个代理接手时不可靠地可用。本文提出了ESAA-Conversational，这是事件溯源代理架构(ESAA)的一个领域特化，用于跨异构代理的共享对话记忆。该方法将可见对话视为本地事件存储：钩子和观察者捕获可见回合，将其规范化为仅追加的activity.jsonl，并确定性地投影出读取模型，如handoff.md、state.md、decisions.md和tasks.json。机械捕获不需要LLM推理；代理仅在使用显式策划时使用判断，通过领域命令记录持久决策和对话任务。公共v1.1.0版本实现了PowerShell CLI，包含init、enable-hooks、sync、project、verify、context、decide和task命令；包括workspace_root隔离和写路径锁文件；并以带有空公共日志的全新包形式分发。一个包含570个开发实验室事件的自引用案例研究表明，异构代理可以通过共享日志协作，而无需直接的代理间通道，同时公共分发通过排除私有对话历史来保护隐私。

Original abstract: Software developers increasingly work with multiple LLM coding agents, switching among tools such as Codex, Grok, Claude Code, and other assistants as context windows fill, sessions end, or a particular agent becomes better suited to a subtask. Each agent, however, persists its conversation in a private and vendor-specific log. The result is conversational state drift: goals, decisions, open tasks, and rationales established with one agent are not reliably available when another agent takes over. This paper presents \emph{ESAA-Conversational}, a domain specialization of Event-Sourcing Agent Architecture (ESAA)~\cite{esaa} for shared conversational memory across heterogeneous agents. The method treats the visible conversation as a local event store: hooks and watchers capture visible turns, normalize them into an append-only \texttt{activity.jsonl}, and deterministically project read models such as \texttt{handoff.md}, \texttt{state.md}, \texttt{decisions.md}, and \texttt{tasks.json}. Mechanical capture does not require LLM inference; agents use judgment only for explicit curation, recording durable decisions and conversational tasks through domain commands. The public v1.1.0 release implements a PowerShell CLI with \texttt{init}, \texttt{enable-hooks}, \texttt{sync}, \texttt{project}, \texttt{verify}, \texttt{context}, \texttt{decide}, and \texttt{task}; includes \texttt{workspace\_root} isolation and a write-path lockfile; and is distributed as a greenfield package with an empty public log. A self-referential case study with 570 development-lab events shows that heterogeneous agents can collaborate through a shared log without a direct agent-to-agent channel, while the public distribution preserves privacy by excluding the private conversational history.

</details>


### [2] [Integrating Heterogeneous Digital Twins in Federated Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22791v1)
*Christian Vergara-Marcillo,Rami Bahsoon,Nikos Tziritas,Wendy Yanez-Pazmino,Panagiotis Oikonomou,Georgios Theodoropoulos*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出联邦节点管理器，一种模块化集成机制，实现异构数字孪生在联邦生态系统中的互操作和协调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数字孪生生态系统研究停留在概念阶段，缺乏实际集成异构DT的方法，需要解决互操作性和运行时协调挑战。

Method: 提出联邦节点管理器，通过受控能力暴露、协议和模式适配、状态和事件交换连接本地DT到联邦环境。

Result: 在智能出行应急响应场景中展示了概念设计和原型实现的可行性。

Conclusion: 联邦节点管理器是服务导向联邦DT生态系统中的使能组件，为分布式DT协作提供基础。

中文摘要：数字孪生（DTs）越来越多地被用于虚拟化不同规模的物理系统，实现监控、仿真和预测以支持决策。然而，虽然单个DT在独立环境中有效，但生态系统规模的部署需要多个自主且分布式的DT跨越系统边界进行协作，尽管它们在建模方法或软件技术上存在差异，这使得互操作性和运行时协调成为关键挑战。尽管联邦数字孪生生态系统已成为一个有希望的方向，但现有研究仍处于概念阶段，提供高层架构的同时，对异构DT的实际集成探索不足。本文提出了联邦节点管理器，一种模块化集成机制，通过受控的能力暴露、协议和模式适配以及及时的状态和事件交换，将本地DT连接到联邦环境以实现协调操作。我们提出了概念设计和原型实现，并在智能出行领域的应急响应场景中展示了其可行性。所提出的机制是更广泛的服务导向联邦DT生态系统中的一个使能组件。

Original abstract: Digital Twins (DTs) are increasingly used to virtualise physical systems at different scales, enabling monitoring, simulation, and predictions to support decision-making. However, while individual DTs are effective in stand-alone settings, ecosystem-scale deployments require multiple autonomous and distributed DTs to cooperate across system boundaries despite differences in modelling approaches or software technologies, making interoperability and runtime coordination critical challenges. Although \textit{Federated Digital Twin Ecosystems} have emerged as a promising direction, existing research remains at the conceptual stage, offering high-level architectures while leaving the practical integration of heterogeneous DTs underexplored. This paper proposes the \textit{Federation Node Manager}, a modular integration mechanism that connects local DTs to a federated environment through controlled capability exposure, protocol and schema adaptation, and timely state and event exchange for coordinated operations. We present a conceptual design and a prototype implementation, and demonstrate their feasibility in the smart mobility domain for emergency response scenarios. The proposed mechanism serves as an enabling component within a broader service-oriented federated DT ecosystem.

</details>


### [3] [From Fragments to Paths: Task-Level Context Recovery for Large Industrial Codebases](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22906v1)
*Jiawei He,Weisong Sun,Mengyu Shi,Jie Jia,Tong Bian,Xikai Yang,Dong Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: DeepDiscovery通过两阶段定位-推理框架，在大型工业代码库中恢复任务级上下文，显著提升文件召回率和下游软件工程任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理大型工业代码仓库时，仅检索局部片段，无法恢复复杂仓库级任务所需的更大范围上下文，导致性能受限。

Method: 采用两阶段“定位-推理”框架：首先定位高置信度任务锚点，然后在多关系仓库结构上在预算约束下恢复更广泛的任务相关上下文。

Result: 在多种评估场景中（方法级、工业仓库、SWE-bench Verified），DeepDiscovery在文件恢复质量和下游SE性能上一致优于多个基线，例如在SWE-bench Verified上解决率提升8.2个百分点。

Conclusion: 更强的任务级仓库理解能力能够显著提升编码代理在复杂软件工程任务上的表现。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在软件工程任务上表现出色，但理解大型工业代码仓库仍然具有挑战性。现有方法通常只检索局部片段，未能恢复复杂仓库级任务所需的更广泛任务相关上下文。我们提出了DeepDiscovery，一种针对大型工业代码库的任务级仓库理解方法。DeepDiscovery采用两阶段“定位-推理”框架，在预算约束下定位高置信度任务锚点，并在多关系仓库结构上恢复更广泛的任务相关上下文。在受控的方法级评估、组织内部工业仓库理解场景以及SWE-bench Verified上的端到端评估中，DeepDiscovery一致地改善了任务相关文件的恢复和下游SE性能。在27个中等规模任务中，DeepDiscovery在没有离线预处理的情况下，在五个代表性基线中实现了最佳文件恢复质量。在来自生产规模集成代码库生态系统的组织内部工业任务中，包括27个中等规模任务和40个大规模任务，DeepDiscovery在多个AI编码系统中提高了完全召回率，在大型子项目上绝对增益从1.6到9.2个百分点不等，在中等规模子项目上从2.5到7.4个百分点不等。在SWE-bench Verified上的受控端到端评估中，配备DeepDiscovery的系统实现了78.6%的解决率，比相应基线高出8.2个百分点。这些结果表明，更强的任务级仓库理解可以提高编码代理在复杂SE任务上的性能。

Original abstract: Large language models have shown strong performance on software engineering (SE) tasks, yet understanding large industrial repositories remains challenging. Existing methods often retrieve only local fragments and fail to recover the broader task-relevant context needed for complex repository-level tasks. We present DeepDiscovery, a task-level repository-understanding method for large industrial codebases. DeepDiscovery uses a two-stage \textit{Location--Inference} framework to localize high-confidence task anchors and recover broader task-relevant context over multi-relational repository structure under budget constraints. Across controlled method-level evaluation, organization-internal industrial repository-understanding scenarios, and end-to-end evaluation on SWE-bench Verified, DeepDiscovery consistently improves task-relevant file recovery and downstream SE performance. On 27 medium-scale tasks, DeepDiscovery achieves the best file recovery quality among five representative baselines without offline preprocessing. On organization-internal industrial tasks from a production-scale integrated codebase ecosystem, including 27 medium-scale tasks and 40 large-scale tasks, DeepDiscovery improves Full Recall Rate across multiple AI coding systems, with absolute gains ranging from 1.6 to 9.2 percentage points on large subprojects and from 2.5 to 7.4 percentage points on medium-scale subprojects. In a controlled end-to-end evaluation on SWE-bench Verified, a system equipped with DeepDiscovery achieves a 78.6\% Solve Rate, outperforming the corresponding baseline by 8.2 percentage points. These results suggest that stronger task-level repository understanding can improve coding-agent performance on complex SE tasks.

</details>


### [4] [EnerInfer: Energy-Aware On-Device LLM Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23001v2)
*Bohua Zou,Nian Liu,Binqi Sun,Matteo Mascherin,Debayan Roy,Yutao Liu,Yu Peng,Ning Jia,Haibo Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: EnerInfer通过动态调整NPU/DDR频率，在不违反QoE的前提下显著提升设备端LLM推理的能效，最高提升65%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统优先优化解码速度，忽略能效；实际中设备端LLM推理存在配置松弛，降低频率可保持QoE并提高能效，但缺少统一的优化框架。

Method: 提出EnerInfer框架，采用模型结构感知预测和排名驱动在线反馈，无需逐模型配置文件和组件级传感器，动态选择QoE满足的高效NPU/DDR频率配置，并结合轻量级有限范围热预测在能效和热约束间切换。

Result: 在手机、笔记本电脑和开发板上分别提升能效65%、12%、24%，且未违反QoE。

Conclusion: EnerInfer有效联合管理了设备端LLM推理的能效、吞吐量和热舒适性，实现了显著能效提升。

中文摘要：设备端大语言模型（LLM）推理因其保护隐私、可靠且经济高效的部署而日益具有吸引力，但其能耗和热成本仍然是一个关键瓶颈。现有系统主要优化解码速度，隐含假设更快的执行总是更好的。我们反而表明，设备端LLM推理通常具有可挖掘的配置松弛：适度降低NPU和内存频率可以保持体验质量（QoE），同时显著提高能效并减少热量。在生产中实现这一机会具有挑战性。最高能效的NPU/DDR设置因模型、推理引擎、平台和运行时条件而异，各配置之间没有稳定的排名。商用设备还缺乏组件级功率感测，外壳温度随请求到达、响应长度和热历史而变化。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了EnerInfer，这是第一个针对LLM工作负载联合管理能效、吞吐量和热舒适性的设备端LLM推理框架。EnerInfer用分离的、模型结构感知的预测和排名驱动的在线反馈取代了每模型配置文件和传感器密集型控制。它预测未见过的LLM在不同NPU/DDR频率设置下的吞吐量和功率，在运行时干扰下选择满足QoE的高效配置，并使用轻量级有限范围热预测在能效优化和热约束的推理之间动态切换。在真实LLM上的评估表明，EnerInfer在手机、笔记本电脑和开发板上分别将能效提高了高达65%、12%和24%，且没有违反QoE。

Original abstract: On-device LLM inference is increasingly attractive for privacy-preserving, reliable, and cost-effective deployment, yet its energy and thermal costs remain a critical bottleneck. Existing systems primarily optimize for decoding speed, implicitly assuming that faster execution is always preferable. We show instead that on-device LLM inference often has exploitable configuration slack: modestly lowering NPU and memory frequencies preserves quality of experience (QoE) while substantially improving energy efficiency and reducing heat.
  Realizing this opportunity in production is challenging. The most energy-efficient NPU/DDR setting varies with the model, inference engine, platform, and runtime conditions, with no stable ranking across configurations. Commercial devices further lack component-level power sensing, and shell temperature evolves with request arrivals, response lengths, and thermal history. To address these challenges, we propose EnerInfer, the first on-device LLM inference framework that jointly manages energy efficiency, throughput, and thermal comfort for LLM workloads. EnerInfer replaces per-model profiling and sensor-heavy control with disaggregated, model-structure-aware prediction and ranking-driven online feedback. It predicts throughput and power for unseen LLMs across NPU/DDR frequency settings, selects QoE-satisfying efficient configurations under runtime interference, and uses lightweight limited-horizon thermal prediction to dynamically switch between energy-optimized and thermally constrained inference. Evaluations on real-world LLMs show that EnerInfer improves energy efficiency by up to 65%, 12%, and 24% on phones, a laptop, and a development board, respectively, without QoE violation.

</details>


### [5] [The EVerest Dataset for Secure Software Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23197v1)
*Sophie Corallo,Debora Grupp,Dominik Fuchß,Jan Keim,Frederik Reiche,Tobias Hey,Anne Koziolek*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了 EVerest 数据集，包含细粒度安全标签的多工件资源，支持安全验证研究，并发现了真实漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据集缺乏同时涵盖需求、架构和代码三层次且带有细粒度安全标签的资源，无法支持端到端安全验证研究。

Method: 基于 EVerest 开源软件栈，手动引出安全需求并标注安全目标，构建细粒度安全元素及追踪链接，整合架构模型、源码和文档。

Result: 数据集包含84个安全需求、1,445个安全元素、追踪链接等，并发现并修复了一个CWE-1295漏洞。

Conclusion: 该数据集为多工件安全验证研究提供了宝贵资源，并展示了其实用性。

中文摘要：从头到尾的安全验证，从需求到架构再到代码，需要跨越所有三种工件类型且带有细粒度安全标签的数据集。现有数据集没有提供这种组合。我们提出了 EVerest 数据集，这是一个基于 EVerest（一个由行业驱动的电动汽车充电站开源软件栈）的多工件资源。该数据集包括 84 个手动引出的安全需求，带有安全目标标注；1,445 个细粒度安全元素（组件、实体、数据、数据流、状态等）；接受窗口；共指关系；以及架构追踪链接。此外，还包括 EVerest 软件架构模型、源代码和自然语言文档。它支持安全需求分类、命名实体识别、架构追踪链接以及设计时或代码级安全验证方面的研究。在数据集创建过程中，我们发现了一个真实的安全弱点（CWE-1295），已向项目维护者披露并随后修复。该数据集是公开可用的。短视频参见 https://youtu.be/pnn1uqpomvQ。

Original abstract: End-to-end security verification, from requirements through architecture to code, requires datasets that span all three artifact types with fine-grained security labels. No existing dataset provides this combination. We present the EVerest dataset, a multi-artifact resource based on EVerest, an industry-driven open-source software stack for electric vehicle charging stations. The dataset includes 84 manually elicited security requirements annotated with security objectives, 1,445 fine-grained security elements (components, entities, data, data flows, states, etc.), acceptance windows, coreferences, and architectural trace links, as well as the EVerest software architecture model, source code, and natural language documentation. It enables research on security requirements classification, named entity recognition, architectural trace linking, and design-time or code-level security verification. During dataset creation, a real security weakness (CWE-1295) was identified, disclosed to the project maintainers, and subsequently fixed. The dataset is publicly available. A short video is available at https://youtu.be/pnn1uqpomvQ.

</details>


### [6] [Generate with CodeXHug: A Dataset to Enhance Model Cards with Code Usage Patterns](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23329v1)
*Stefano Palombo,Claudio Di Sipio,Juri Di Rocco,Davide Di Ruscio*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了CodeXHug数据集，收集了HuggingFace上PTMs在GitHub中的实际使用代码模式，并通过统计分析和聚类提取代表性模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多PTMs在实际项目中未被充分使用，且缺乏解释性代码模式，增加了使用难度。

Method: 从HuggingFace转储开始，筛选带有标签和模型卡的PTMs，再到GitHub查询实际使用，收集了7,325个模型和20,545个Python文件，然后通过统计分析和聚类提取代码模式。

Result: 收集了7,325个不同模型和20,545个Python文件，构成CodeXHug数据集。

Conclusion: CodeXHug可以用于提取代表性代码使用模式，支持开发者使用PTMs。

中文摘要：预训练模型（PTMs）在软件工程社区中越来越受欢迎。模型仓库（例如HuggingFace）促进了它们的使用，这些仓库收集、存储和维护了大量的PTMs。然而，这些模型在实际项目中的实际采用情况仍然是一个未解决的问题，即许多模型被用于玩具项目或仅仅是HF仓库的镜像。此外，大多数可用的模型卡和包含其使用关键信息的文本文档不包括解释性代码模式，从而增加了新手的难度。因此，我们看到需要有一个与PTMs相关的精选代码库，以支持有兴趣在项目中使用它们的开发者和实践者。在本文中，我们提出了CodeXHug，这是一个经过精选的HuggingFace PTMs数据集，这些模型在Github生态系统中被利用，并附带相关的代码使用模式。从最新的HF转储开始，我们首先进行数据整理，收集带有标签和模型卡的PTMs。然后，查询Github平台以找到所识别PTMs的实际使用情况，得到了7,325个不同的模型和20,545个Python文件。为了展示CodeXHug的具体应用，我们提出了一个使用场景，通过统计分析和聚类技术应用于相关代码片段，提取特定PTMs的代表性代码使用模式。

Original abstract: Pre-trained models (PTMs) are becoming increasingly popular in the software engineering community. Their usage is facilitated by model repositories, e.g., HuggingFace, which collect, store, and maintain a wide range of PTMs. However, the actual adoption of these models in real-world projects is still an open question, i.e., many of them are used in toy projects or simply as a mirror for the HF repository. In addition, most of the available model cards and textual documents that contain critical information about their usage do not include explanatory code patterns, thus increasing the difficulty for newcomers. Thus, we see the need for a curated codebase related to PTMs to support developers and practitioners who are interested in using them in their projects.
  In this paper, we present CodeXHug, a curated dataset of HuggingFace PTMs exploited in the Github ecosystem and the related code usage patterns. Starting from the latest HF dump, we first conduct a data curation to collect PTMs with a tag and a model card. Then, the Github platform has been queried to find actual usages of the identified PTMs, resulting in 7,325 different models and 20,545 Python files.
  To demonstrate a concrete application of CodeXHug, we propose a usage scenario focused on extracting representative code usage patterns for specific PTMs through a statistical analysis and clustering techniques applied to relevant code snippets.

</details>


### [7] [Automated Semantic Fault Localization in SysML v2: A Human-in-the-Loop Framework Using Knowledge-Graph Augmented LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23395v1)
*Haitham Al-Shami,Rohail Malik,Riku Ala-Laurinaho,Jari Vepsäläinen,Raine Viitala*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种人在环框架，结合微调小型语言模型和领域知识图谱，自动识别和修复SysML v2模型中的语义错误，在车辆系统领域验证，修复率从<3%提升至>91%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编译器无法检测保持语法正确但违反领域规则的语义错误，这些错误会导致后期集成失败，因此需要自动识别和修复此类错误的方法。

Method: 结合微调的小型语言模型（SLM）和领域知识图谱；知识图谱编码物理兼容性规则，指导合成训练数据生成，并在推理时增强模型；SLM输出统一差异补丁定位故障和提供修复建议。

Result: 在1,184个测试样本上，微调将语义故障修复率从不到3%提高到超过91%，补丁输出减少令牌长度超过60%。

Conclusion: 该框架为AI辅助模型验证提供了实用路径，补充现有MBSE工具，并通过人在环保留人类判断。

中文摘要：SysML v2的文本语法支持基于编译器的模型结构和语言一致性验证。然而，保持语法正确但违反领域规则的语义错误无法通过编译器检测。这些错误可能在设计过程中传播，并在后期表现为代价高昂的集成失败。本文提出了一种人在环框架，用于自动识别和修复此类错误。它结合了微调的小型语言模型（SLM）和编码系统元素间物理兼容性规则的领域知识图谱。知识图谱还通过系统性地引入合理的领域违规来指导合成训练数据的生成，并在推理时增强模型，使修复建议基于有效的工程约束。我们使用车辆系统领域演示了该框架，其中知识图谱捕捉了机械、电气、流体和信号接口之间的关系。两个SLM，Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B和DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B，被微调以输出统一差异补丁，定位故障并为工程师审查提供候选修复，在设计过程中保留人类判断。对1,184个测试样本的评估表明，微调将语义故障修复率从不到3%提高到超过91%，基于补丁的输出将令牌长度减少了60%以上。该框架为AI辅助模型验证提供了一条实用路径，补充了现有的MBSE工具。

Original abstract: SysML v2's textual syntax enables compiler-based validation of model structure and language conformance. However, semantic mistakes that preserve syntactic validity but violate domain rules cannot be detected through compilers. These errors can propagate through the design process and surface late as costly integration failures. This paper presents a human-in-the-loop framework for identifying and repairing such errors automatically. It combines a fine-tuned Small Language Model (SLM) with a domain knowledge graph encoding physical compatibility rules between system elements. The knowledge graph also guides the generation of synthetic training data by systematically introducing plausible domain violations, and augments the model at inference time to ground repair suggestions in valid engineering constraints. We demonstrate the framework using the vehicle systems domain, where the knowledge graph captures the relationships between the mechanical, electrical, fluid, and signal interfaces. Two SLMs, Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B and DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B, are fine-tuned to output unified diff patches that localize faults and present candidate repairs for engineer review, preserving human judgment in the design process. Evaluation of 1,184 test samples shows that fine-tuning improves semantic fault repair from less than 3% to more than 91%, with patch-based output reducing token length by over 60%. The framework offers a practical path toward AI-assisted model verification that complements existing MBSE tools.

### [8] [The Prevalence and Impact of Licenses in Open Software Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23445v1)
*Mahmoud Jahanshahi,Bogdan Vasilescu,Audris Mockus*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 分析了超过1亿个软件项目的许可证分布及变更影响，发现大多数项目无许可证，宽松型许可证占比增加，但限制型许可证更易被保留，且许可证变更对不同语言生态系统影响相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解软件项目许可证的分布状况及其变更对项目活动的影响。

Method: 识别超过1亿个软件项目的许可证类型，分析其分布随时间的变化，并比较从限制型转向宽松型许可证前后一年内的项目活动。

Result: 大多数项目无许可证；宽松型许可证占主导且比例上升；限制型许可证更易保留；C语言生态系统偏好限制型许可证；许可证变更对C语言（活动减少）和Python（活动增加）影响相反。

Conclusion: 许可证类型流行度随时间发生剧烈变化，且许可证变更对项目活动的影响因语言生态系统而异。

中文摘要：公开可用的源代码的使用方式由其许可证决定。许可证（或其缺失）反过来影响项目可以重用哪些代码以及其代码如何被（重）使用，还可能影响外部参与和项目的整体活动。我们旨在更好地理解许可证分布的整体状况以及在不同语言生态系统中的分布，并调查许可证变更是否与项目产出的显著变化相关。为此，我们识别了超过1亿个软件项目的许可证和许可证类型，发现大多数项目不包含任何许可证，宽松型许可证占许可证的大多数，并且宽松型许可证在所有许可证中的比例随时间增加。然而，限制型许可证更可能被保留。不同语言生态系统之间存在很大差异，C语言强烈偏好限制型许可证。对许可证变更影响的分析比较了采用初始和最终许可证后一年内的活动，结果显示从限制型到宽松型许可证的变更因生态系统而异。C语言生态系统在从限制型转向宽松型许可证时活动减少，而Python则显示活动增加。我们的结果揭示了许可证类型流行度随时间发生的剧烈变化，并发现许可证变更的影响可能因语言生态系统而异，产生相反的效果。

Original abstract: The terms of how publicly available source code can be used are dictated by its license. The license (or its absence), in turn, affects what code the project may reuse and how its code can be (re)used and may also affect external participation and overall activity of the project. We aim to better understand the general state of license distribution overall and within language ecosystems and to investigate if license changes are associated with a noticeable variations of project output. To accomplish that we identify licenses and license types for over 100M software projects and find that most do not contain any license, that permissive licenses represent the bulk of most licenses, and that permissive licensing is representing an increasing proportion of all licenses over time. Restrictive licenses are more likely to be retained, however. There is a great variation among language ecosystems with C-language strongly favoring restrictive licenses. The analysis of license change impact comparing activity within one year of the adoption of the initial and final licenses shows that the change from restrictive to permissive license varies with the ecosystem. C-language ecosystems show reduced activity while Python shows increased activity when comparing restrictive to permissive license transition. Our results demonstrate dramatic changes in license type prevalence over time and find that the effects of license changes may have opposite effects depending on the language ecosystem.

</details>


### [9] [An Automated Framework for Input Alphabet Construction in Stateful Protocol Implementation Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23464v1)
*JiongHan Wang,WenChao Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文利用大语言模型自动生成协议状态机学习的输入字母表，并采用小批量增量学习策略降低开销，实验证明了其能发现安全漏洞和语义缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手工定义输入字母表限制了状态机学习的完整性，难以捕获异常非规范消息，导致遗漏语义缺陷。

Method: 采用大语言模型解析协议消息布局，按结构化变异规则生成候选符号，自动覆盖有效/无效消息空间；引入小批量增量学习策略重用已有自动机。

Result: 在实用协议栈上重现了已知漏洞并发现了新的语义缺陷，部分已被开发者确认和修补。

Conclusion: 提出的自动字母表生成和增量学习方法实用有效，能提升状态机学习的缺陷发现能力。

中文摘要：作为一种对有状态协议实现进行普遍分析的技术，状态机学习存在一个核心瓶颈，即依赖于手工制作的输入字母表。手动定义字母表本质上限制了输入探索的完整性，使得难以捕获异常的不符合规范的消息，从而遗漏潜在的语义缺陷。本文针对状态机学习的自动输入字母表生成，以突破上述限制。我们采用大语言模型解析协议消息布局，并按照结构化变异规则生成候选输入符号，自动覆盖有效和无效的消息空间，消除对人工协议专业知识的依赖。考虑到字母表持续增长带来的开销增加，我们引入了一种小批量增量学习策略，在合并新的字母表条目时重用现有学习到的自动机。对实际协议栈的综合实验表明，我们的方法能够重现现有的安全漏洞并识别新的语义缺陷。其中一些新发现的问题已被开发者确认和修补，证明了我们提出方法的实用性和有效性。

Original abstract: As a prevalent analytical technique for stateful protocol implementations, state machine learning suffers from a core bottleneck stemming from handcrafted input alphabets. Manual alphabet definition inherently limits the completeness of input exploration, making it difficult to capture anomalous non-conformant messages and consequently missing latent semantic defects.
  In this paper, we target automatic input alphabet generation to break the above limitation for state machine learning. We adopt large language models to parse protocol message layouts and produce candidate input symbols following structured mutation rules, which automatically covers valid and invalid message spaces and eliminates reliance on manual protocol expertise.
  Considering the rising overhead brought by continuously growing alphabets, we introduce a mini-batch incremental learning strategy to reuse existing learned automata when incorporating new alphabet entries. Comprehensive experiments on practical protocol stacks indicate our approach can reproduce existing security vulnerabilities and identify novel semantic bugs. A subset of these newly discovered issues has been confirmed and patched by developers, proving the practicability and effectiveness of our proposed method.

### [10] [Ensuring Open Source Integrity: The Intersection of Copy-Based Reuse and License Compliance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23495v1)
*Mahmoud Jahanshahi,Bogdan Vasilescu,Audris Mockus*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 基于复制的代码重用网络显示，开源软件中39.4%的项目组合存在潜在许可证不合规风险，且依赖分析仅能检测2.43%的复制重用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 源代码的复制重用难以追踪，导致许可证合规性问题，需要量化整个开源生态系统中潜在的许可证不合规程度。

Method: 利用World of Code基础设施构建基于复制的代码重用网络，并采用回归模型分析许可证对复制的影响。

Result: 发现宽松许可证（MIT、Apache）代码重用可能性高；copyleft混合；公共领域许可证反而降低重用；39.4%项目组合存在潜在不合规；仅2.43%复制重用可通过依赖分析检测。

Conclusion: 现有依赖追踪工具在检测基于复制的代码重用方面存在严重局限性，需要更好的方法来评估许可证合规性。

中文摘要：与其他创造性作品一样，源代码受版权保护。所有者可以许可该作品，例如允许复制和其他类型的使用，甚至可以对违反许可证的行为提起法律诉讼。然而，源代码可以通过微妙的方式被重用，例如通过没有明确包管理器依赖关系的复制，这使得难以推理潜在的许可证不合规行为。利用近似于全部开源软件的World of Code基础设施，在本文中我们创建了一个基于复制的代码重用网络，映射项目间的直接复制，并用它来量化整个开源生态系统中潜在的许可证不合规程度。此外，我们估计回归模型以理解代码复制是否受源项目许可证的影响，如果是，它如何随其他项目特征变化。我们发现，具有宽松许可证（如MIT和Apache）的仓库中的代码在编程语言间显示出更高的重用可能性。相反，copyleft许可证（如GPL）表现出混合效应。公共领域许可证尽管旨在允许无限制使用，但与较低的基于复制的重用可能性相关。广泛的潜在许可证不合规似乎伴随着基于复制的重用，39.4%的项目组合处于潜在不合规风险中，特别是在许可证不明确或缺失时。我们的发现表明，通过基于复制的网络检测到的重用中只有2.43%可以通过依赖分析发现，突出了现有依赖跟踪工具在捕获基于复制的重用方面的局限性。

Original abstract: As other creative work, source code is protected by copyright. The owner can license the work, e.g., to permit copy and other kinds of use, and even start legal proceeding against license violators. However, source code can be reused in subtle ways, e.g., via copying without explicit package manager dependencies, making it hard to reason about potential license noncompliance. Using the World of Code infrastructure approximating the entirety of open source software, in this paper we create a copy-based code reuse network mapping direct copying across projects, and use it to quantify the extent of potential license noncompliance across the entire open source ecosystem. In addition, we estimate regression models to understand whether code copying is affected by the origin project's license, and, if so, how it varies with other project characteristics. We find that code in repositories with permissive licenses, such as MIT and Apache, shows higher likelihood of reuse across programming languages. In contrast, copyleft licenses, like the GPL, exhibit mixed effects. Public domain licenses, despite their aim of allowing unrestricted use, are associated with lower likelihood of copy-based reuse. A widespread potential license noncompliance appears to accompany copy-based reuse, with 39.4% of project combinations at potential noncompliance risk, particularly when licenses are unclear or absent. Our findings reveal that only 2.43% of reuse detected through the copy-based network was discoverable via dependency analysis, highlighting the limitations of existing dependency-tracking tools in capturing copy-based reuse.

</details>


### [11] [Source-Free Detection and Impact Analysis of Compiler Optimization Problems in Mobile Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23512v1)
*Han Hu,Xiaoheng Xie,Bo Sun,Jian Gu,Gang Fan,Li Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出OptDetect框架，通过分析二进制文件检测低优化级别编译的原生库，发现30.5%的库存在该问题，修复后可显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动应用中低优化级别编译的原生库导致性能下降，但现有工具难以检测，且开发者未意识到该问题。

Method: 提出OptDetect框架，通过二进制反汇编、块级分类和加权得分聚合，无需源码即可检测二进制文件中的编译器优化级别问题。

Result: 在受控和真实数据集上分别达到93.0%和81.9%准确率；对21972个库检测发现30.5%使用低优化；修复后CPU指令减少10-63%，性能投诉减少42%，评分提升0.14。

Conclusion: 低优化级别的原生库普遍存在且影响严重，自动化检测工具OptDetect有效，同时需要行业级优化标准。

中文摘要：移动应用程序经常遭受性能问题，例如帧率下降、过热和过高的功耗。虽然开发者优化算法和调试代码，但一个关键的瓶颈往往被忽视：以低优化级别（O0/O1而非O2/O3）编译的原生库。由于这些库在功能上无错误地执行，由此产生的性能下降在生产应用程序中仍然隐藏，影响数百万用户。我们提出	extsc{OptDetect}，一个无源码框架，可直接从应用程序二进制文件检测编译器优化问题，无需源代码或构建元数据。	extsc{OptDetect}通过二进制反汇编、块级分类和加权得分聚合的流水线处理单个二进制文件中的混合优化级别，在受控数据集上达到93.0%的准确率，在真实数据集上达到81.9%的准确率。将	extsc{OptDetect}应用于来自830个顶级Google Play应用的21,972个原生库，我们发现30.5%的库使用低优化级别，影响91.7%的应用。通过对12个生产应用（6个商业，6个开源）的案例研究，我们证明修复检测到的问题可将商业应用的CPU指令减少10-63%（中位数：20.5%），开源应用减少15-58%（中位数：32%），性能投诉中位数减少42%，评分中位数增加0.14分。进一步调查揭示了一个先前被忽视的根本原因：广泛使用的第三方库本身以低优化级别分发，在一个主要仓库的1,073个库中有49.7%存在此问题。这些发现凸显了自动化检测工具和行业级优化标准的必要性。

Original abstract: Mobile apps frequently suffer from performance issues such as frame drops, overheating, and excessive power consumption. While developers optimize algorithms and debug code, a critical bottleneck often goes unnoticed: native libraries compiled with low optimization levels (O0/O1 instead of O2/O3). Because these libraries execute without functional errors, the resulting performance degradation remains hidden in production apps, affecting millions of users.
  We present \textsc{OptDetect}, a source-free framework that detects compiler optimization problems directly from app binaries without requiring source code or build metadata. \textsc{OptDetect} handles mixed optimization levels within a single binary through a pipeline of binary disassembly, chunk-level classification, and weighted score aggregation, achieving 93.0\% accuracy on controlled datasets and 81.9\% on real-world datasets. Applying \textsc{OptDetect} to 21,972 native libraries from 830 top-ranked Google Play apps, we find that 30.5\% of libraries use low optimization levels, affecting 91.7\% of apps.
  Through case studies on 12 production apps (6 commercial, 6 open-source), we demonstrate that fixing detected issues reduces CPU instructions by 10-63\% (median: 20.5\%) for commercial apps and 15-58\% (median: 32\%) for open-source apps, with performance complaints decreasing by a median of 42\% and ratings increasing by a median of 0.14 points. Further investigation reveals a previously overlooked root cause: widely-used third-party libraries are themselves distributed at low optimization levels, with 49.7\% of 1,073 libraries in a major repository exhibiting this problem. These findings highlight the need for automated detection tools and industry-wide optimization standards.

</details>


### [12] [From Task-Guided Conversational Graphs to Goal-Oriented Dialogue Runtimes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23797v1)
*Mariano Garralda-Barrio*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出GODR设计模式，通过将目标等作为一等运行时对象来解决复杂多目标对话的连续性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编排框架无法应对用户多个相互依赖目标导致的对话不连续问题。

Method: 引入面向目标的对话运行时（GODR），将目标、任务框架、生命周期状态、失效规则和恢复契约作为一等对象，并将执行委托给现有框架。

Result: 论文形式化了问题并提出了架构选择标准，但未提供实证性能评估，而是将其作为未来工作。

Conclusion: GODR适用于复杂、多领域、可中断的对话场景，而非简单引导过程。

中文摘要：图和多智能体编排框架使得大规模语言模型（LLM）工作流的生产部署变得实用，但它们本身并不能解决用户维护多个相互依赖目标时的对话连续性。这篇概念性系统论文专注于该设计空间中高复杂度的极端情况，即目标可以被其他目标中的操作暂停、恢复、修订和失效。我们引入了面向目标的对话运行时（GODR），这是一种框架中性的设计模式，它将目标、任务框架、生命周期状态、失效规则和恢复契约视为一等运行时对象，同时将有限执行委托给图运行时、智能体、工具或应用程序编程接口（API）。GODR并非作为简单引导过程中工作流图的替代品；它旨在用于复杂的、多领域的、可中断的对话，在这些对话中，目标连续性无法仅通过智能体身份、聊天历史或执行图位置可靠地恢复。本文形式化了该问题，提出了运行时对象和架构选择标准，并将评估框定为未来实证验证的议程，而非作为测量性能声明。

Original abstract: Graph and multi-agent orchestration frameworks make production large language model (LLM) workflows practical, but they do not by themselves solve conversational continuity when users maintain several interdependent objectives. This conceptual systems paper focuses on the high-complexity end of that design space, where goals can be suspended, resumed, revised, and invalidated by actions in other goals. We introduce the Goal-Oriented Dialogue Runtime (GODR), a framework-neutral design pattern that treats goals, task frames, lifecycle state, invalidation rules, and resumption contracts as first-class runtime objects while delegating bounded execution to graph runtimes, agents, tools, or application programming interfaces (APIs). GODR is not proposed as a replacement for workflow graphs in simple guided processes; it is intended for complex, multi-domain, interruptible conversations where objective continuity cannot be recovered reliably from agent identity, chat history, or execution-graph position alone. The paper formalizes the problem, proposes runtime objects and architecture-selection criteria, and frames evaluation as an agenda for future empirical validation rather than as a measured performance claim.

</details>


### [13] [JupOtter: Cell-Level Bug Detection in Jupyter Notebooks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23877v1)
*Lukas Ottenhof,Thibaud Lutellier*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了JupOtter，一个针对Jupyter Notebooks的错误检测系统，包括新的分词策略、单元格级错误预测和大型标注数据集，在多数数据集上优于现有方法。

Conclusion: JupOtter为Jupyter Notebooks提供了有效的错误检测能力，尤其通过细粒度单元格级分析和专用数据集提升了性能。

中文摘要：Jupyter Notebooks是一种日益流行的编码环境，广泛应用于许多领域，尤其是基于Python的数据科学和科学计算。最初用于原型设计和交互式探索，现在笔记本越来越多地用于开发更复杂的程序，导致GitHub等平台上存在错误的笔记本数量迅速增加。为了应对这一趋势，我们提出了JupOtter，一个专门为Jupyter Notebooks设计的错误检测系统。JupOtter具有三个新颖贡献：（1）一种保留单元格结构的笔记本特定分词策略，（2）一种单元格级错误预测技术，以及（3）一个新的标记数据集OtterDataset，包含超过21,000个注释了细粒度单元格级错误检测的笔记本。JupOtter在三个评估数据集中的两个上实现了超越静态分析器和大型语言模型的单元格级错误检测F1分数。

Original abstract: Jupyter Notebooks are an increasingly popular coding environment used across many domains, especially in Python-based data science and scientific computing. Originally used for prototyping and interactive exploration, notebooks are increasingly used to develop more complex programs, leading to a rapid rise in buggy notebooks on platforms like GitHub. To address this trend, we present JupOtter, a bug detection system designed specifically for Jupyter Notebooks. JupOtter features three novel contributions: (1) a notebook-specific tokenization strategy that preserves cell structure, (2) a cell-level bug prediction technique, and (3) a new labeled dataset, OtterDataset, containing over 21,000 notebooks annotated for fine-grained cell-level bug detection. JupOtter achieves cell-level bug detection F1 scores that surpass static analyzers and large language models in two out of three evaluation datasets.

### [14] [Domain-Driven Design in Practice: A Mining Study of Maintenance and Evolution in Open-Source Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23984v1)
*Weixing Zhang,Bowen Jiang,Yuhong Fu,Haowei Cheng,Mario Herb,Anne Koziolek*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究通过对GitHub上开源DDD仓库的大规模实证分析，揭示了DDD战术构建块的分布、演化及其与软件维护质量的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管DDD在软件工程中影响广泛，但缺乏大规模实证证据支持其实际使用和维护效果，因此需要系统性研究。

Method: 使用GitHub搜索API收集DDD相关仓库，结合自动关键词过滤和人工评估，通过四个研究问题分析构建块的静态分布、演化、边界违规及维护活动关联。

Result: 该研究预期将揭示DDD构建块的分布模式、演化趋势、边界违规的规模及其与维护活动的关系。

Conclusion: 这些研究问题共同追溯了开源DDD项目的完整维护和演化生命周期，为未来的DDD工具支持和方法论改进建立了实证基础。

中文摘要：领域驱动设计（DDD）是一种有影响力的软件开发方法论，它通过战术构建块（如实体、值对象、聚合和仓储）围绕业务领域复杂性来组织软件。尽管它在软件工程中非常突出，但关于DDD如何被实践、如何演变以及如何与开源项目中的软件维护质量相关的大规模实证证据仍然缺乏。本研究提出了一项预注册的实证调查，调查开源 GitHub 仓库中 DDD 战术构建块的分布、演化和维护影响，以回应最近系统文献综述中确定的对大规模实证评估的需求。我们将使用搜索 API 从 GitHub 收集与 DDD 相关的仓库，应用自动关键词过滤和手动相关性评估，并通过四个研究问题分析所得数据集，涵盖：（RQ1）DDD 构建块在各仓库类型中的静态分布和共同使用情况，（RQ2）它们在提交历史中的纵向演化，（RQ3）有界上下文边界违规（DDD 采用中的主要技术挑战，尚未大规模量化）的程度及维护影响，以及（RQ4）DDD 仓库中维护活动与构建块变更或有界上下文违规之间的时间关联。这些研究问题共同追溯了开源 DDD 项目的完整维护和演化生命周期，并为未来的 DDD 工具支持和方法论改进建立了实证基础。

Original abstract: Domain-Driven Design (DDD) is an influential software development methodology that structures software around business domain complexity through tactical building blocks such as Entities, Value Objects, Aggregates, and Repositories. Despite its prominence in software engineering, large-scale empirical evidence on how DDD is practiced, how it evolves, and how it relates to software maintenance quality in open-source projects remains scarce. This study presents a pre-registered empirical investigation of the distribution, evolution, and maintenance implications of DDD tactical building blocks in open-source GitHub repositories, addressing the call for large-scale empirical evaluations identified in a recent systematic literature review. We will collect DDD-related repositories from GitHub using the Search API, apply automated keyword filtering and manual relevance assessment, and analyze the resulting dataset through four research questions covering: (RQ1) the static distribution and co-usage of DDD building blocks across repository types, (RQ2) their longitudinal evolution over commit history, (RQ3) the extent and maintenance implications of Bounded Context boundary violations (the primary technical challenge in DDD adoption, unquantified at scale), and (RQ4) the temporal association between maintenance activities and building block churn or Bounded Context violations in DDD repositories. Together, these RQs trace the full maintenance and evolution lifecycle of open-source DDD projects and establish an empirical foundation for future DDD tool support and methodology refinement.

### [15] [Closed-loop Auto Research for Molecular Property Prediction: Discovering and Certifying Generalizable Improvements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22731v1)
*Jingjie Ning,Xiaochuan Li,Ji Zeng,Chenyan Xiong,Guolin Ke*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 闭环自动研究框架，LLM agent编辑代码与表示并获取外部证据，可迁移至自动代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 在分子性质预测中，闭环自动研究通过分离验证和保留测试，发现特征、模型和外部证据轴的迁移性因套件而异，且策展数据存在过拟合风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究闭环自动研究的动作空间（特征、模型、外部证据）是否能在分子性质预测的多个小端点上产生超越验证信号的泛化改进。

Method: 在三个基准套件的36个端点上，通过文件级消融锁定将增益归因于特定轴，对每个配置在保留测试上评分，并设计路由管道选择最佳验证轴。

Result: 路由管道在保留测试上达到0.013-0.042的增益，可迁移轴因套件而异；模型搜索和策展数据存在非迁移迹象；策展外部数据仅对特定端点有效且需污染过滤；自动化机器学习控制未能复现代理代码干预。

Conclusion: 将发现与保留认证分离是闭环系统优化代理的领域无关教训，分子性质预测中可迁移改进有限且需谨慎评估泛化。

中文摘要：闭环自动研究将自动化机器学习从固定数据集拟合扩展到改变研究工作流程，语言模型代理编辑表示和模型代码并获取外部证据。分子性质预测涵盖许多小型端点。我们询问这个动作空间是否能够产生超越用于选择它们的验证信号的泛化改进。我们隔离了三个自动研究轴：特征、模型和外部证据，在文件级消融锁定下，将每个增益归因于相对于强基线的某个轴。在三个基准套件的36个端点上，我们每个选定的配置在搜索从未读取其标签的保留测试上评分一次。一个路由管道，取每个端点的最佳验证轴，在保留测试上达到了0.013、0.011和0.042的正增益，可迁移的轴因套件而异：TDC上为数据，Polaris上为模型，MoleculeNet上为特征和模型。最大的模型搜索增益从验证集的0.041下降到测试集的0.003，而策展数据达到0.022但在测试集上为负0.019，这是两个不可迁移的迹象。策展的外部数据将保留的CYP2C9-底物性能提高了0.17，半衰期提高了0.08，通过一个污染过滤器，拒绝与测试结构重叠64%至89%的同源文件，这对于迁移是必要但不充分的。一个匹配试验的自动化机器学习控制未能重现代理的代码级模型干预，达到0.006 vs 0.042，并且该管道在共享训练分割上与一个84M参数的预训练3D模型保持竞争力。实验保持在分子性质预测范围内，但将发现与保留认证分开是任何优化代理以保留数量的闭环系统的领域无关的教训。

Original abstract: Closed-loop Auto Research extends automated machine learning from fixed-dataset fitting to changing the research workflow, with language-model agents editing representations and model code and acquiring external evidence. Molecular property prediction spans many small endpoints. We ask whether this action space yields improvements generalizing beyond the validation signal selecting them.
  We isolate three Auto Research axes, features, models, and external evidence, under a file-level ablation lock attributing each gain to one axis over a strong baseline. Across 36 endpoints in three benchmark suites we score each selected configuration once on a held-out test whose labels the search never read. A routed pipeline taking each endpoint's best validation axis reaches positive held-out gains of 0.013, 0.011, and 0.042, the transferable axis differing by suite, data on TDC, model on Polaris, feature and model on MoleculeNet. The largest model-search gain falls from 0.041 on validation to 0.003 on test, while curated data reaches 0.022 but negative 0.019 on test, two non-transfer signatures. Curated external data raises held-out CYP2C9-substrate performance by 0.17 and half-life by 0.08, admitted through a contamination filter rejecting same-source files overlapping 64 to 89 percent of test structures, necessary but not sufficient for transfer. A matched-trial automated machine learning control did not reproduce the agent's code-level model intervention, reaching 0.006 against 0.042, and the pipeline stays competitive with an 84M-parameter pretrained 3D model on the shared training split.
  The experiments stay within molecular property prediction, but separating discovery from held-out certification is a domain-agnostic lesson for any closed-loop system optimising a proxy for a held-out quantity.

</details>


### [16] [GroundEval: A Deterministic Replacement for LLM-as-Judge in Stateful Agent Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22737v2)
*Jeffrey Flynt*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: GroundEval 是一个无需评判员的框架，通过记录智能体的搜索、获取和引用轨迹来检测其是否使用了正确证据，能发现 LLM 评判员无法察觉的虚假证据路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 作为评判员的评估方法无法检测智能体是否使用了错误证据，导致看似合理的回答可能基于无效证据路径。

Method: GroundEval 使用领域配置生成问题，记录智能体回答的完整轨迹，并针对沉默、视角和反事实三种失败模式进行评分。

Result: 案例表明智能体频繁使用无效证据路径，最终答案和评判员评估无法检测此类问题，而 GroundEval 可暴露并量化。

Conclusion: GroundEval 提供了一种可检查的、基于证据的评估方式，能有效识别智能体在推理中依赖错误证据的失败模式。

中文摘要：在让智能体在真实环境中运行之前，你能证明它使用了正确的证据吗？GroundEval 将这个问题转化为一个确定性测试，测试智能体搜索、获取、引用和被允许访问的内容。在一个案例研究中，两个前沿的 LLM 评判员给一个看似合理的智能体回答打了 0.85 分及以上的高分。但追踪记录显示了一个不同的故事：该智能体从未检索到其回答所依赖的工件，导致 GroundEval 得分为 0.000。我们提出了 GroundEval，一个无需评判员的框架，用于评估智能体在基于证据、时间限制和访问控制下的表现。GroundEval 使用领域配置生成问题，让智能体选择如何回答，然后对最终答案和产生答案的记录轨迹进行评分。该基准针对 LLM 作为评判员难以检测的三种失败模式：智能体在声称不存在之前是否检查过，是否仅根据行为者在相关时间可获得的证据进行推理，以及是否使用了正确的因果机制而非似是而非的机制。这些对应三个轨道：沉默、视角和反事实。GroundEval 揭示了看似合理的答案何时建立在无效的证据路径上，并生成结构化的逐问题诊断，将工具活动与智能体的轮次叙述相结合，使每个得分都可以检查而不仅仅是报告。我们的案例研究表明，这种失败模式是普遍而非例外的，是最终答案和基于评判员的评估在构造上无法检测到的。

Original abstract: Before letting an agent operate over real context, can you prove it used the right evidence? GroundEval turns that question into a deterministic test of what the agent searched, fetched, cited, and was permitted to access. In one case study, two frontier LLM judges scored a plausible agent response 0.85 and higher. But the trace told a different story: the agent had never retrieved the artifact its answer depended on, yielding a GroundEval score of 0.000.
  We introduce GroundEval, a judge-free framework for evaluating agents against grounded, time-bounded, and access-controlled evidence. GroundEval uses a domain configuration to generate questions, lets the agent choose how to answer, and then scores both the final answer and the recorded trajectory that produced it. The benchmark targets three failures that LLM-as-judge evaluation struggles to detect: whether an agent checked before claiming absence, reasoned only from evidence available to the actor at the relevant time, and used the correct causal mechanism rather than a plausible one. These correspond to three tracks: Silence, Perspective, and Counterfactual. GroundEval exposes when plausible answers rest on invalid evidence paths, and produces structured per-question diagnostics that pair tool activity with the agent's turn-level narration, making each score inspectable rather than merely reported. Our case studies suggest this failure mode is common rather than exceptional, one that final-answer and judge-based evaluation cannot detect by construction.

</details>


### [17] [The Origins of Stochasticity: Comprehensive Investigations on Uncertainty Quantification for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22792v1)
*Xiang-Jun Ou,Shuang Liang,Xin-Yu Hu,Rong-Hao Huang,Jing Wang,Shao-Qun Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM不确定性量化综述，对agent置信度评估有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种细粒度不确定性分类法，将LLM不确定性归因于输入、参数、令牌和解码过程，并分类现有UQ方法。通过评估21种方法发现，基于共识的方法效果最佳，且模型规模与不确定性呈负相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统不确定性分类无法捕捉LLM生成的多组件和多阶段特性，且难以评估UQ方法有效性，因此需要更系统的分类和评估框架。

Method: 提出细粒度不确定性分类（输入级、参数级、令牌级、解码过程），将UQ方法分为贝叶斯、集成、基于共识和单次传递四类，并构建综合评估框架。

Result: 实验表明UQ方法效果因任务和生成设置而异；基于共识的方法（Deg、EigV）最优；模型规模越大，不确定性越低，存在标度律。

Conclusion: 本研究弥合了不确定性理论来源与LLM部署之间的差距，提供了系统量化不确定性的实用工具。

中文摘要：近年来，大型语言模型（LLM）的进步实现了复杂的推理和内容生成，但其固有的随机性对确保预测可靠性构成了重大挑战。虽然传统的不确定性分类范式（如偶然不确定性和认知不确定性的二分法）提供了概念基础，但它们通常无法捕捉LLM生成的多组件和多阶段特性，也难以评估各种不确定性量化（UQ）方法的有效性。在本文中，我们提出了一种细粒度不确定性分类法，将LLM不确定性系统地归因于输入级、参数级、令牌级和解码过程来源。相应地，我们将现有的UQ方法分为贝叶斯方法、集成方法、基于共识的方法和单次传递方法。此外，我们引入了一个涵盖多样化生成设置和指标的综合评估框架。我们在三个主要LLM系列（包括Qwen3、Llama 3.2和DeepSeek-V3）上，针对TriviaQA、GSM8K和HumanEval等基准，对21种典型UQ方法进行了实证评估。我们的实验结果表明：（i）UQ方法的有效性对任务类型和生成设置敏感；（ii）基于共识的方法（如Deg和EigV类型）始终优于其他UQ方法；（iii）更大的模型规模与更低的不确定性估计相关，这表明LLM不确定性存在一种经验标度律。这项工作弥合了理论基础与实际部署之间的差距，为系统量化LLM应用中的不确定性提供了一种多功能诊断工具。

Original abstract: Recent advancements in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled sophisticated reasoning and content generation, yet their inherent stochasticity poses significant challenges for ensuring predictive credibility. While traditional uncertainty taxonomy paradigms, such as the dichotomy of aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties, provide conceptual foundations, they often fail to capture the multi-component and multi-stage nature of LLM generation and struggle to evaluate the effectiveness of various Uncertainty Quantification (UQ) methods. In this paper, we propose a granular uncertainty taxonomy that systematically attributes LLM uncertainty into input-level, parameter-level, token-level, and decoding-process sources. Correspondingly, we categorize existing UQ methods into Bayesian, ensemble, consensus-based, and single-pass approaches. Furthermore, we introduce a comprehensive evaluation framework covering diverse generation settings and metrics. We empirically evaluate 21 typical UQ methods across three prominent LLM families, including Qwen3, Llama 3.2, and DeepSeek-V3, on benchmarks such as TriviaQA, GSM8K, and HumanEval. Our experimental results demonstrate that (i) the effectiveness of UQ methods is sensitive to task types and generation settings; (ii) consensus-based methods, typed Deg and EigV, consistently outperform other UQ approaches; and (iii) larger model scales correlate with lower uncertainty estimates, suggesting an empirical scaling law for LLM uncertainty. This work bridges the gap between theoretical origins and practical deployment, providing a versatile diagnostic tool for systematically quantifying uncertainty in LLM applications.

</details>


### [18] [A Formula-Driven Survey and Research Agenda for On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22793v1)
*Bowen Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: On-policy蒸馏的综述，涉及反馈驱动更新，可迁移至agent自我改进。

TL;DR: 本文对在线策略蒸馏（OPD）进行了综述，提出了一个公式驱动的分类法，区分了时间信用和词汇路由两种机制，并由此衍生出GAE-OPD和CR-OPD等方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究OPD作为反馈到更新问题而非单一损失族，以系统组织核心方法并明确其有效性因素。

Method: 通过两条路径（直接分布损失和策略梯度风格的对数比更新）构建分类法，区分时间信用与词汇路由机制，并推导偏界及新方法。

Result: 揭示了OPD有效性依赖于状态兼容性、支持构建、时间信用等多种因素；提出了GAE-OPD和CR-OPD等具体变体。

Conclusion: 将诊断、失败机制、案例等映射到统一变量，并提供行动性指南和报告检查表。

中文摘要：在线策略蒸馏（OPD）训练一个LLM，该LLM作用于由当前或最近的学生策略诱导的状态：学生生成完整或部分轨迹，教师或自我教师在其生成的上下文下对得到的令牌进行评分，并将密集的对数概率、logit或分布信号转换为训练后更新。本调查将OPD作为一个反馈到更新的问题而非单个损失族进行研究。我们通过两条路径——直接分布损失和策略梯度风格的对数比更新——开发了一个公式驱动的分类法，并利用它来组织核心方法、验证器或结果导向的混合方法、工业报告、框架实现、失败模式以及在明确证据边界下的稳定化方案。该分类法表明，OPD的有效性不仅取决于KL方向或教师访问，还取决于状态兼容性、支持构建、时间信用、词汇级概率路由、门控和权重以及正则化。我们进一步区分了在采样令牌OPD稳定性讨论中经常混淆的两种机制。时间信用询问教师-学生对数比回报应如何对轨迹中的采样动作进行加权；词汇路由询问当负反馈抑制了一个采样令牌时，概率质量应向何处移动。这一区分产生了即时、剩余回报、折扣和基线校正估计量的偏界，推动了GAE-OPD作为对数比回报的基于价值的假设，并推动了反事实路由OPD（CR-OPD）将概率质量路由到教师支持、学生可达的替代方案。最后，我们将可操作性诊断、失败机制、案例研究、开放问题和一个报告检查表映射到相同的反馈到更新变量上。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains an LLM on states induced by the current or recent student policy: the student generates complete or partial rollouts, a teacher or self-teacher scores the resulting tokens under their generated contexts, and dense log-probability, logit, or distributional signals are converted into post-training updates. This survey studies OPD as a feedback-to-update problem rather than a single loss family. We develop a formula-driven taxonomy from two routes -- direct distributional losses and policy-gradient-style log-ratio updates -- and use it to organize core methods, verifier- or outcome-guided hybrids, industrial reports, framework implementations, failure modes, and stabilization recipes under explicit evidence boundaries. The taxonomy shows that OPD effectiveness depends not only on KL direction or teacher access, but also on state compatibility, support construction, temporal credit, vocabulary-level probability routing, gates and weights, and regularization. We further separate two mechanisms often conflated in sampled-token OPD stability discussions. Temporal credit asks how teacher-student log-ratio returns should weight sampled actions across a rollout; vocabulary routing asks where probability mass should move when negative feedback suppresses a sampled token. This distinction yields bias boundaries for immediate, return-to-go, discounted, and baseline-corrected estimators, motivates GAE-OPD as a value-based hypothesis for log-ratio returns, and motivates Counterfactual Routed OPD (CR-OPD) for routing probability mass toward teacher-supported, student-reachable alternatives. We close by mapping actionability diagnostics, failure mechanisms, case studies, open problems, and a reporting checklist onto the same feedback-to-update variables.

</details>


### [19] [Measuring Behavior Portability in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22797v1)
*Tianjia Dong,Nadav Kunievsky,James A. Evans*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 测量LLM行为可移植性，对agent跨环境泛化评估有启发。

TL;DR: LLM在结构等效但表面不同的决策环境中行为可移植性差，提出的框架量化了这种损失，实验发现显著损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于基准测试的评估脆弱，因为LLM对决策环境的表面呈现敏感，需要量化行为可移植性以确保评估的可靠性。

Method: 提出形式化框架：在源环境数据上拟合可解释行为模型，在留出的目标环境中评估样本外预测性能，使用与损失无关的度量给出最坏情况边界，并对比直接在目标数据上训练的基准。

Result: 在七个经典经济决策问题的受控实验中，观察到显著且系统的可移植性损失。

Conclusion: LLM在一个决策环境中获得的行为特征不能可靠地转移到结构等效但表面不同的替代环境中，因此套件式评估需要谨慎解释。

中文摘要：大型语言模型正越来越多地被部署为自主决策者，但它们在结构上等效（即具有相同的支付相关结构但表面呈现不同）的决策环境中表现出的行为映射可能存在显著差异。这种敏感性使得基于基准测试集的评估变得脆弱，并引发了一个关于行为可移植性的基本问题：在一个决策环境中学习到的行为映射在多大程度上能对另一个具有相同潜在激励结构的环境提供信息？我们引入了一个形式化框架来衡量这一属性。我们的协议在从一组源环境中汇集的数据上拟合一个可解释的行为模型，并在一个留出的目标环境中评估其样本外预测性能，与直接在目标数据上训练的基准进行比较。可移植性通过一个与损失无关的度量来量化，该度量提供了目标环境中诱导的预测-动作映射性能的最坏情况边界。在涵盖七个经典经济决策问题的受控实验中，我们记录了显著且系统的可移植性损失，这表明在一个决策环境中获得的LLM行为特征不能可靠地转移到结构上等效的替代环境中。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as autonomous decision makers, yet the behavioral mapping they exhibit can vary substantially across decision environments that are payoff-equivalent by construction-environments that share identical payoff-relevant structure but differ in surface presentation. This sensitivity renders suite-based evaluation fragile and raises a fundamental question of behavioral portability: how well does a behavioral mapping learned in one decision environment informative on another that preserves the same underlying incentive structure? We introduce a formal framework to measure this property. Our protocol fits an interpretable behavioral model on data pooled from a set of source environments and evaluates its out-of-sample predictive performance in a held-out target environment, benchmarking against an oracle trained directly on target data. Portability is quantified via a loss-agnostic measure that delivers worst-case bounds on the performance of the induced prediction-action mapping in the target environment. In controlled experiments spanning seven canonical economic decision problems, we document substantial and systematic portability losses, suggesting that behavioral characterizations of LLMs obtained in one decision environment cannot be assumed to transfer reliably to structurally equivalent alternatives.

### [20] [Active Inference as the Test-Time Scaling Law for Physical AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22813v1)
*Omar Hashash,Christo Kurisummoottil Thomas,Walid Saad,Merouane Debbah,Karl Friston,Adeel Razi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出active inference作为agent的test-time scaling law，通用agent推理方法。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于主动推理的物理AI测试时缩放定律，通过变分推理动态更新策略，实现泛化并提升效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缩放定律受限于模型大小和训练数据，无法应对物理AI在真实世界中遇到的非平稳和未知场景。

Method: 基于主动推理第一性原理，将测试时策略更新建模为软贝叶斯推理，利用变分推理最小化自由能边界，同时更新策略和世界模型。

Result: 在自动驾驶仿真中，该方法优于Q学习和贝叶斯强化学习，泛化鲁棒，推理效率提升36%以上。

Conclusion: 该缩放定律随真实世界经验扩展，使物理AI能够在测试时通过推理实现泛化，具有生物学解释和实际应用价值。

中文摘要：本文提出了一种针对物理人工智能（AI）代理的新型测试时缩放定律。该缩放定律使物理AI代理能够在测试时利用其世界模型进行推理，从而在未见场景中实现泛化。该缩放定律基于主动推理的第一性原理，该原理赋予代理在现实世界中生存的通用目标，其具体任务目标被包含在该通用目标之下。主动推理通过提供推理来解决当代理遇到训练分布之外的未知情况时产生的预测误差，从而实现在非平稳环境中的泛化。所提出的缩放定律通过在测试时利用这种推理动态更新代理的策略来捕捉这一过程。该策略更新被建模为一个软贝叶斯推理过程，其中关于策略的信念通过使用减少允许策略下预期预测误差的推理作为似然函数进行更新。得到的后验策略具有生物学解释，恢复了在测试时调动大脑基底神经节和前额叶皮层的缩放机制。为了解决这个解析困难的问题，提出了一种最小化自由能边界的变分推理解决方案。该解决方案扩展了学习能力，通过在测试时解决的新实例来强化策略和世界模型，从而实现超越训练的学习。与受模型大小和训练数据限制的现有缩放定律不同，所提出的解决方案随着物理AI代理在真实世界中的连续经验而扩展。在自动驾驶任务上的仿真结果表明，所提出的解决方案优于无模型Q学习和基于模型的贝叶斯强化学习，在实现对未见场景的鲁棒泛化的同时，推理效率提高了36%以上。

Original abstract: In this paper, a novel test-time scaling law for physical artificial intelligence (AI) agents is introduced. This scaling law enables physical AI agents to reason with their world models to generalize in unforeseen scenarios at test time. The derived scaling law is grounded in the first principle of active inference, which equips agents with the general objective to survive in the real world, under which their specific task objectives are subsumed. Active inference achieves this by providing the reasoning to resolve prediction errors that arise when the agent encounters unforeseen situations outside its training distribution, enabling generalization in non-stationary environments. The proposed scaling law captures this by dynamically updating the agent's policy with this reasoning at test time. This policy update is modeled as a soft Bayesian inference process in which beliefs about the policy are updated using the reasoning that reduces expected prediction errors under allowable policies as a likelihood. The resulting posterior policy admits a biological interpretation, recovering the scaling mechanism that engages the brain's basal ganglia and prefrontal cortex at test time. To solve this analytically intractable problem, a variational inference solution minimizing free energy bounds is developed. This solution extends to enable learning beyond training by reinforcing new instances, resolved at test time, in both the policy and world model. Unlike existing scaling laws constrained by model size and training data, the derived solution scales with the continuous real-world experience of a physical AI agent. Simulation results on an autonomous driving task demonstrate that the proposed solution outperforms model-free Q-learning and model-based Bayesian reinforcement learning, achieving robust generalization to unforeseen scenarios while improving inference efficiency by over 36%.

### [21] [Finding the Evidence: Discovering Decision-Supporting Tokens for On-Policy Reasoning Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22830v1)
*Jinwei Xiao,Zhuowen Han,Yueqing Sun,Zhengxi Lu,Yuxin Liu,Zhiyuan Yao,Wentao Chen,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出决策-证据感知的推理蒸馏方法，可迁移至agent推理能力提升。

TL;DR: 提出DEAR方法，通过分别识别推理链中的决策和证据知识，实现更有效的在线策略蒸馏，在数学和代码任务上显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线策略蒸馏方法只捕捉推理链中的决策知识，而忽略了证据知识，导致实质性知识无法传递。

Method: DEAR方法通过学生熵识别决策，然后利用隐藏状态与决策锚点的余弦相似度发现支持证据，并通过教师-学生差异增强以优先处理知识差距。

Result: 在数学和代码基准的三个学生-教师配置中，DEAR相比标准OPD在竞赛数学上提升+2.5pp，代码生成上提升+5.7pp。

Conclusion: DEAR通过同时传递决策和证据知识，有效提升了在线策略蒸馏的性能，验证了两种知识区分的重要性。

中文摘要：在线策略蒸馏通过密集的令牌级监督传递推理能力，但可传递信号的性质仍不清楚。我们发现推理链包含两种需要不同发现机制的知识：决策（在哪里分支），通过学生的不确定性显现；以及证据（证明决策合理性的中间步骤），隐藏在学生自信但错误的的位置上。当前方法仅捕获了决策；证据令牌中的实质性知识仍未传递。我们提出了DEAR（决策-证据感知推理蒸馏），该方法首先通过学生熵识别决策，然后通过隐藏状态与决策锚点的余弦相似度发现其支持证据，并通过教师-学生差异进行增强，以优先处理最大的知识差距。在数学和代码基准上的三种学生-教师配置中，DEAR始终优于标准OPD，在竞赛数学上提升高达+2.5个百分点，在代码生成上提升高达+5.7个百分点。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation transfers reasoning ability through dense token-level supervision, yet the nature of the transferable signal remains unclear. We discover that reasoning chains contain two types of knowledge that require different discovery mechanisms: decisions (where to branch), which surface through student uncertainty, and evidence (intermediate steps that justify decisions), which hides in positions where the student is confident yet wrong. Current methods capture only decisions; the substantive knowledge in evidence tokens remains untransferred. We propose DEAR(Decision-Evidence Aware Reasoning Distillation), which first identifies decisions via student entropy, then discovers their supporting evidence through hidden-state cosine similarity to decision anchors, boosted by teacher-student divergence to prioritize the largest knowledge gaps. Across three student-teacher configurations on math and code benchmarks, DEAR consistently outperforms standard OPD, with up to +2.5pp on competition math and +5.7pp on code generation.

### [22] [RaMem: Contextual Reinstatement for Long-term Agentic Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22844v1)
*Wei Yang,Bryce Kan,Shixuan Li,Li Li,Yuehan Qin,Jiate Li,Paul Bogdan,Jesse Thomason*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出面向LLM agent的长周期记忆框架RaMem，解决上下文遗忘问题，核心agent记忆方法

TL;DR: RaMem通过上下文重建将检索到的记忆片段转化为可验证证据，解决LLM长期记忆中的上下文崩溃问题，平均F1提升超10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长期记忆系统仅注重检索，但检索到的记忆片段因脱离上下文而无法提供有效证据，导致上下文崩溃问题。

Method: 提出RaMem框架，包含证据锚定、召回条件归纳、有效性感知检索和上下文保留合成四个阶段，将记忆片段与查询上下文对齐。

Result: 在多个长期记忆基准上，RaMem相对强基线平均F1提升超过10%。

Conclusion: RaMem有效缓解上下文崩溃，提升LLM智能体在长期交互中的记忆利用效果。

中文摘要：长期记忆对于在扩展交互和不断变化的任务上下文中运行的LLM智能体变得越来越重要。最近的记忆系统使过去的经验更加持久、紧凑和可检索，但仅凭检索并不能确保记忆为当前查询提供有效证据。当经验被压缩成可重用的片段时，如果不同情境的记忆涉及重复出现的实体或用户状态，它们可能看起来同样相关。我们将这种失败称为上下文崩溃：记忆失去了判断其是否为当前查询提供有效证据所需的周围上下文。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了智能体记忆的上下文重建（RaMem），这是一个将检索到的记忆片段转化为可在上下文中验证的证据的框架。RaMem通过四个协调阶段运行：（i）证据锚定将每个记忆锚定在其原始事件条件中，特别是事件时间、提及时间、会话跨度以及参与者；（ii）召回条件归纳推导出查询隐含的证据条件；（iii）有效性感知检索使用这些条件优先考虑上下文兼容的记忆，同时保留内容相关的候选者作为回退证据；（iv）上下文保留合成使所选记忆的结构化上下文对生成器可用。在长期记忆基准上的实验表明，与强大的记忆基线相比，RaMem持续提高了性能，在多个主干上的平均F1增益超过10%。

Original abstract: Long-term memory has become increasingly important for LLM agents that operate across extended interactions and evolving task contexts. Recent memory systems have made past experiences more persistent, compact, and retrievable, but retrieval alone does not ensure that a memory provides valid evidence for the current query. When experiences are compressed into reusable fragments, memories from different situations may appear equally relevant if they involve recurring entities or user states. We refer to this failure as context collapse: memories lose the surrounding context needed to judge whether they provide valid evidence for the current query. To address this problem, we propose Contextual Reinstatement for Agentic Memory (RaMem), a framework that turns retrieved memory fragments into contextually verifiable evidence. RaMem operates through four coordinated stages: (i) evidence anchoring grounds each memory in its original episodic conditions, especially event time, mention time, session span, and participants; (ii) recall condition induction derives the evidence conditions implied by the query; (iii) validity-aware retrieval uses these conditions to prioritize context-compatible memories while retaining content-relevant candidates as fallback evidence; and (iv) context-preserved synthesis keeps the selected memories' structured context available to the generator. Experiments on long-term memory benchmarks show that RaMem consistently improves performance over strong memory baselines, with average F1 gains of more than 10% across several backbones.

</details>

Original abstract: Agentic artificial intelligence (AI) systems are beginning to assist, accelerate, and partially automate scientific discovery, performing tasks that span literature synthesis, code generation, data analysis, hypothesis proposal, and model criticism. We argue that this transition is qualitative rather than incremental, and that suitably designed multi-agent systems may evolve from passive computational tools into ``AI scientists'' that can expand the hypothesis-generating and verification capacity of science. Such systems must be developed and deployed within a scientific ecosystem fit for purpose: institutions must be redesigned for verification, accountability, interpretability, and dual-use safety. We sketch how multi-agent architectures, illustrated by the prototype framework \textit{Denario}, accelerate the discovery cycle and traverse model spaces beyond human reach; examine what this implies for authorship, peer review, and the enduring role of human scientists; and close with recommendations for governing AI as an epistemic actor rather than a mere instrument.

### [24] [CLI-Universe: Towards Verifiable Task Synthesis Engine for Terminal Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22883v1)
*Zhanbo Hua,Yifan Yao,Weihao Xie,Yongchi Zhao,Minghao Liu,Ruizhi Qiu,Zhewei Huang,Zun Wang,Yiyan Ji,Yunhai Ye,Letian Zhu,Xinping Lei,Han Li,Zhiyuan Ma,Zili Wang,Zhaoxiang Zhang,Jiaheng Liu*
