### [54] [When Confidence Takes the Wrong Path: Diagnosing Retrieval-State Lock-In in RAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22728v1)
*Sahib Julka*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 诊断RAG中检索状态锁定问题，提出可审计的置信度规则，对agent可靠性设计有启发。

TL;DR: 本文识别并命名了RAG系统中的“检索状态锁定”问题，即因检索状态缺陷导致答案虚假一致，并提出了将置信度分解为答案、证据和检索状态的诊断方法，实验表明该方法能有效发现错误，但以牺牲覆盖率为代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒不确定性方法在RAG中因忽略检索状态缺陷而误将答案一致性视为高置信度，导致虚假置信，亟需识别该问题并给出可测量的诊断和缓解方案。

Method: 通过将RAG置信度分解为答案表面、检索证据和检索状态三个对象，在可检查的KG-RAG系统中测量共识盲区，并设计可审计决策规则：仅当三者均判定低风险时才接受答案。

Result: KG-RAG中42%错误和密集检索中59%错误具有零答案离散度；分解后的决策规则达到91.9%精确率（vs 69.7%全部接受），但覆盖率仅7.7%；临床校准域自动评估达100%精确率。

Conclusion: RAG置信度是对象特定的，当答案一致时需追问流水线哪部分不可信；分解方法能提高精度但降低覆盖率，需结合具体应用权衡，且仍要人工验证。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）系统的可信度不仅仅取决于其返回的答案，然而许多黑盒不确定性方法仍然将采样答案之间的一致性视为置信度。当重复采样基于相同的缺陷检索状态时，这种推断就会失败。该状态可能是空的，模型转而依赖参数记忆，或者由一致但错误的邻域填充。在这两种情况下，答案之所以一致，是因为错误是稳定的。这一问题在部署的RAG中已被认识到，但一直缺乏名称、可测量的特征和普遍性界限。我们提供了这三者。我们将这种失败命名为检索状态锁定（retrieval-state lock-in），并通过分离单个置信度得分所混淆的三个对象来进行诊断：答案表面、检索证据和检索状态本身。在一个可检查的、本体引导的知识图谱RAG（KG-RAG）系统中，跨越六个问答快照，我们直接测量了共识盲区：每问题五个样本时，42%的KG-RAG错误和59%的密集检索错误具有零答案离散度，因此一致性无法用于排序，而证据和检索状态检查仍能标记出其中大部分。这种分解支持一种可审计的决策规则：仅当答案、证据和检索检查都认为低风险时才接受答案，达到了91.9%的合并精确率，而全部接受率为69.7%。代价是覆盖率：仅认证了7.7%的答案为低风险。在临床校准领域，在自动评判器下达到了100%的精确率；这是领域内自动标注的上限，并非临床安全声明，仍需人工验证。RAG中的置信度是对象特定的：当答案一致时，有用的问题是流水线的哪一部分不可信。

Original abstract: The trustworthiness of a retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) system depends on more than the answer it returns, yet many black-box uncertainty methods still read agreement among sampled answers as confidence. That inference fails when repeated samples condition on the same defective retrieval state. The state may be empty, with the model falling back on parametric memory, or populated by a coherent but wrong neighbourhood. In either case, the answers agree because the error is stable. The problem is recognised in deployed RAG, but it has lacked a name, a measurable signature, and a prevalence bound. We supply all three. We name the failure retrieval-state lock-in and diagnose it by separating the three objects a single confidence score conflates: the answer surface, the retrieved evidence, and the retrieval state itself. In an inspectable, ontology-guided knowledge-graph RAG (KG-RAG) system across six question-answering snapshots, we measure the agreement blind spot directly: at five samples per question, 42% of KG-RAG errors and 59% of dense-retrieval errors carry zero answer dispersion, so agreement has nothing to rank, while evidence- and retrieval-state checks still flag most of them. The decomposition supports an auditable decision rule: accepting an answer only when answer, evidence, and retrieval checks all agree that it is low-risk reaches 91.9% pooled precision against a 69.7% accept-all rate. The cost is coverage: it certifies only 7.7% of answers as low-risk. On the clinical calibration domain it reaches 100% precision under an automated judge; this is an in-domain automated-label upper bound, not a clinical safety claim, and still needs human validation. Confidence in RAG is object-specific: when answers agree, the useful question is which part of the pipeline to distrust.

</details>


### [55] [StatABench: Dataset and Framework for Evaluating Statistical Analysis Capabilities of LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22977v1)
*Youxin Zhu,Yixuan Ding,Peng Lai,Longyue Wang,Bingyi Jing,Guanhua Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM统计分析基准，涉及agent框架评估，对构建agent benchmark有参考。

TL;DR: 提出StatABench基准测试系统评估LLM的统计分析能力，发现即使最强模型在封闭式题目仅68.6%，开放式任务约61.9分，表明LLM在统计分析上仍有显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM统计分析评估基准在范围和格式上有限，无法全面衡量LLM的复杂统计推理与工具使用能力。

Method: 构建StatABench，包含404道多格式封闭式题目和30个开放式建模任务；采用LangChain MCP框架、数据科学智能体和LLM-as-Judge评估协议进行系统评估。

Result: GPT-5.1在Stat-Closed上68.6%，最佳开源模型60.6%；Stat-Open上最佳智能体框架平均61.86分。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在工具推理、方法决策和端到端建模上仍与可靠统计分析存在显著差距，需要进一步改进。

中文摘要：统计分析是一个广泛而复杂的领域，既需要领域知识也需要工具熟练度。虽然先前的工作已经评估了大型语言模型（LLM）在该领域的能力，但现有基准在范围和格式上仍然有限。为弥补这一差距，我们引入了StatABench（统计分析基准），这是一个旨在系统评估LLM统计分析能力的基准。StatABench包含两个互补组件：Stat-Closed包含覆盖18个统计主题的404道题目，格式多样（选择题、填空题、决策题和实际应用题）；Stat-Open包含30个改编自专业竞赛的复杂开放式建模任务。我们使用LangChain MCP框架和多个数据科学智能体评估了多种LLM，并通过经过验证的LLM-as-Judge协议评估Stat-Open的解决方案。实验表明，即使是GPT-5.1在Stat-Closed上也仅达到68.6%，而最好的开源模型达到60.6%。在Stat-Open上，最优智能体框架平均得分为61.86。这些结果揭示了当前LLM与可靠统计分析之间的差距，突出了在基于工具的推理、方法决策和端到端统计建模方面持续存在的挑战。

Original abstract: Statistical analysis is a broad, complex field requiring both domain knowledge and tool proficiency. While prior work has evaluated large language models (LLMs) in this domain, existing benchmarks remain limited in scope and format. To bridge this gap, we introduce StatABench (Statistical AnalysisBenchmark), a benchmark designed to systematically assess LLMs' statistical analysis capabilities. StatABench comprises two complementary components: Stat-Closed, containing 404 questions across 18 statistical topics in multiple formats (multiple-choice, fill-in-the-blank, decision-making, and practical application), and Stat-Open, featuring 30 complex open-ended modeling tasks adapted from professional competitions. We evaluate diverse LLMs using the LangChain MCP framework and multiple data science agents, and assess Stat-Open solutions via a validated LLM-as-Judge protocol. Experiments show that even GPT-5.1 achieves only 68.6% on Stat-Closed, while the best open-source model reaches 60.6%. On Stat-Open, the top agent framework scores 61.86 on average. These results reveal the gap between current LLMs and reliable statistical analysis, highlighting persistent challenges in tool-grounded reasoning, methodological decision-making, and end-to-end statistical modeling.

</details>


### [56] [PhoneBuddy: Training Open Models for Agentic Phone Use](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23049v2)
*Zhengyang Tang,Xin Lai,Pengyuan Lyu,Xinyuan Wang,Tianyi Bai,Chenxin Li,Yiduo Guo,Huawen Shen,Yuxuan Liu,Junyi Li,Zhengyao Fang,Yang Ding,Yi Zhang,Weinong Wang,Xingran Zhou,Liang Wu,Fei Tang,Sunqi Fan,Shangpin Peng,Zheng Ruan,Anran Zhang,Benyou Wang,Ji-Rong Wen,Rui Yan,Chengquan Zhang,Han Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 训练agent执行手机操作，提出混合环境RL训练方法，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: PhoneBuddy通过结合真实和模拟环境训练，显著提升了手机智能体任务成功率，表明模拟环境是真实环境的有效补充。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 训练可靠的手机使用智能体面临真实环境难以重置和验证、模拟环境不够真实的挑战。

Method: 提出PhoneBuddy，结合真实应用环境与模拟应用环境PhoneWorld，先进行共享SFT，再分别进行纯真实RL和混合RL训练。

Result: 150项真实手机任务成功率：SFT后36.67%，纯真实RL后40.67%，混合RL后45.33%；AndroidWorld上从60.3%升至77.2%再升至83.2%。

Conclusion: 模拟训练不是真实RL的替代品，而是可扩展、可重置的补充；短期任务增益大，长期跨应用工作流仍是挑战。

中文摘要：手机正在成为通用型智能体的重要执行界面，但训练用于可靠手机使用的开放模型仍然困难重重，因为部署时真正重要的环境——运行真实应用程序的真实设备——速度慢、有状态、有副作用，且难以重置或验证，而可扩展的模拟环境仅能近似真实行为。我们提出了PhoneBuddy，一种用于智能体手机使用的训练方案和开放模型系列，它结合了真实应用环境与模拟应用环境PhoneWorld，后者从真实GUI使用结构中重构出可运行的模拟应用。PhoneBuddy首先从两个环境中收集的轨迹构建一个共享的有监督微调阶段，然后比较纯真实应用强化学习与跨两个环境的混合强化学习。在涵盖应用、小程序以及跨应用工作流的真实手机150任务人工评估中，任务成功率从有监督微调后的36.67%提升到纯真实应用强化学习的40.67%，再到混合强化学习的45.33%。在AndroidWorld上，同样的进展从60.3%上升到77.2%再到83.2%。这些结果表明，模拟应用训练不是真实应用强化学习的替代品，而是可扩展、可重置且可自动检查的交互的补充来源。增益在应用和小程序任务上最为显著，而长期跨应用工作流仍然是一个重要的开放挑战。

Original abstract: Phones are becoming an important execution surface for general-purpose agents, but training open models for reliable phone use remains difficult because the environment that matters at deployment, real devices running real apps, is slow, stateful, side-effectful, and hard to reset or verify, while scalable mock environments only approximate real behavior. We present PhoneBuddy, a training recipe and open-model line for agentic phone use that combines a real-app environment with a mock-app environment, PhoneWorld, which reconstructs runnable mock apps from real GUI usage structure. PhoneBuddy first builds a shared supervised fine-tuning stage from trajectories collected in both environments, then compares real-app RL against mixed RL across both environments. Across a 150-task human evaluation on real phones spanning apps, mini-apps, and cross-app workflows, task success rate improves from 36.67\% after supervised fine-tuning to 40.67\% after real-app RL and 45.33\% after mixed RL. On AndroidWorld, the same progression rises from 60.3\% to 77.2\% to 83.2\%. These results show that mock-app training is not a replacement for real-app RL, but a complementary source of scalable, resettable, and automatically checked interaction. The gains are strongest on app and mini-app tasks, while long-horizontal cross-app workflows remain an important open challenge.

### [57] [When Does Intrinsic Self-Correction Help? A Task-Sensitive Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23196v1)
*Elroy Stav,Dvir Berlowitz,Maayan Orner,Sarit Kraus*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 任务敏感的自我修正分析，对agent自我反思机制的理解有贡献。

TL;DR: 内在自我修正的效果高度依赖任务结构，在适合的任务中能带来性能提升，但并非普遍可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究质疑内在自我修正的可靠性，作者希望从任务敏感角度探究其在何种条件下有效以及运作机制。

Method: 针对不同任务（验证显式约束、复杂推理、文字游戏中的竞争策略）设计实验，在多个基准和模型上测试自我修正的效果。

Result: 当任务结构支持验证、重新审视或提供第二意见等修订模式时，自我修正能持续提升模型性能。

Conclusion: 自我修正应被视为一种任务依赖的推理时策略，其有效性取决于修订阶段在特定任务中的作用，而非通用的改进方法。

中文摘要：内在自我修正旨在通过提示模型在无外部反馈的情况下重新审视其初始答案来改进大语言模型的输出。近期研究质疑了这种方法的可靠性，表明模型通常难以判断其初始回答是否正确。在这项工作中，我们采用一种任务敏感视角来看待自我修正。我们不是询问它在一般情况下是否有效，而是考察自我修正可能通过不同机制运作的场景：验证显式约束、重新审视复杂推理过程，或在文字游戏任务中为竞争策略提供第二意见。跨多个基准和模型，我们发现当底层任务结构有利于这些修订模式时，自我修正能够带来一致的性能提升。这些结果表明，自我修正最好被理解为一种任务依赖的推理时策略，其有用性取决于修订阶段在给定任务中所能扮演的角色，而非作为改进初始模型输出的统一可靠方法。

Original abstract: Intrinsic self-correction (SC) aims to improve large language model outputs by prompting a model to revisit its own initial answer without external feedback. Recent studies have questioned the reliability of this approach, showing that models often struggle to judge whether their initial responses are correct. In this work, we take a task-sensitive view of SC. Rather than asking whether it works in general, we examine settings where SC may operate through different mechanisms: verifying explicit constraints, revisiting a complex reasoning process, or providing a second opinion over competing strategies in word-game tasks. Across multiple benchmarks and models, we find that SC can yield consistent performance gains when the underlying task structure facilitates these modes of revision. These results suggest that SC is best understood as a task-dependent inference-time strategy whose usefulness depends on the role the revision stage can play in a given task, rather than as a uniformly reliable method for improving initial model outputs.

### [58] [MuPPET: A Benchmark for Contextual Privacy of LLM Assistants in Multi-Party Conversations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23217v1)
*Elena Sofia Ruzzetti,Cornelius Emde,Sangdoo Yun,Seong Joon Oh,Martin Gubri*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多方对话中LLM助手的上下文隐私基准，关注多智能体环境下的隐私风险。

TL;DR: 现有隐私基准仅覆盖一对一场景，本文提出MuPPET基准，发现LLM在多方对话中泄露更多隐私，现有防御效果有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文隐私基准只针对单对话者设置，无法测量多方对话中隐私泄露的额外风险。

Method: 提出MuPPET基准，通过构建多方对话场景并测试模型在群聊中的隐私泄露行为。

Result: 模型在多方设置中泄露显著多于一对一设置；前沿模型脆弱，小型开源模型更甚；现有防御仅部分有效且降低效用。

Conclusion: 多方隐私风险被严重低估，需开发专门针对多方场景的隐私防护方法，尤其是解决参与者追踪问题。

中文摘要：LLM代理越来越多地部署在多方环境中，代表个体用户处理敏感的个人数据，例如在群聊中。当这样的代理披露私人信息时，它会立即到达每个群成员。这种风险在结构上比一对一设置更难控制，因为每一条私人信息都必须适合群组中的每个接收者。然而，所有现有的上下文隐私基准只考虑单对话者设置，留下了多方隐私风险未被测量。我们引入了MuPPET（多方隐私暴露测试），一个用于多方对话中的上下文隐私基准。我们的实验表明，模型在多方设置中泄露的信息比一对一评估所暗示的要多得多。前沿模型是脆弱的，而较小的开源模型（通常因处理敏感数据而更受本地部署青睐）则更加脆弱。现有的上下文隐私防御仅提供部分保护，降低效用，并且没有解决根本的参与者追踪问题。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly deployed in multi-party environments, handling sensitive personal data on behalf of individual users, for instance in group chats. When such an agent discloses private information, it reaches every group member at once. This risk is structurally harder to control than in one-to-one settings, as every piece of private information must be appropriate for every recipient in the group. Yet all existing contextual privacy benchmarks consider only single-interlocutor settings, leaving multi-party privacy risks unmeasured. We introduce MuPPET (Multi-Party Privacy Exposure Testing), a benchmark for contextual privacy in multi-party conversations. Our experiments show that models leak substantially more in multi-party settings than one-to-one evaluations suggest. Frontier models are vulnerable, and smaller open-weights models, often preferred for local deployment with sensitive data, even more so. Existing contextual privacy defences offer only partial protection, degrade utility, and do not resolve the underlying party-tracking problem.

Original abstract: The emergence of Large Reasoning Models has introduced exceptionally long Chain-of-Thought traces, creating a transparency burden where critical logic is often buried under massive procedural text. To address this, we present ReasoningLens, an open-source framework designed for the hierarchical visualization and diagnostic auditing of complex reasoning chains. ReasoningLens addresses information necropsy by: (1) structuring traces into interactive hierarchies that separate high-level strategy from low-level execution; (2) leveraging an agentic auditor for automated error detection and tool-augmented verification; and (3) synthesizing systemic reasoning profiles to reveal model-specific blind spots. By transforming unstructured walls of text into actionable insights, ReasoningLens provides a modular foundation for interpreting, debugging, and optimizing the next generation of reasoning-centric AI.

Original abstract: Enterprise agents increasingly operate inside workspaces: they read heterogeneous files, invoke tools, and deliver business artifacts. ### [62] [When Retrieval Metrics Mislead: Measuring Policy Signal in Long-Horizon Tool-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23937v1)
*Tianyu Ding,Juan Pablo De la Cruz Weinstein*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究长程工具使用agent中检索信号对策略分类的影响，对agent检索设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: 精确匹配召回率低估了检索器对下游策略分类的效用；实验显示检索到的策略子句与金牌子句的宏F1相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在tau-bench中使用Qwen2.5-3B/7B分类器，比较金牌策略和检索到的策略子句对宏F1的影响。

Result: 检索到的子句宏F1为0.58，金牌子句为0.60，差异不显著；控制组更低。

Conclusion: 精确匹配召回率可能低估策略效用，应使用检索到的策略进行循环评估。

中文摘要：精确匹配检索召回率通常被用作衡量检索器是否为下游决策模型提供有用策略上下文的代理指标。我们在tau-bench中使用Qwen2.5-3B/7B分类器测试了这一代理指标在行动前策略分类中的表现。在金牌策略条件下，紧凑的结构化状态经过调优后，相比原始轨迹的宏F1提升了0.13-0.17。然后，我们将基准指定的策略子句替换为从决策时刻上下文中检索到的排名最高的子句。尽管确切的管辖策略子句仅在对7%的航空公司状态排名第一时被检索到，但主要的3B分类器在使用检索到的子句时获得了0.58的宏F1，而使用金牌子句时为0.60（差异=-0.02，任务簇95%置信区间[-0.23,+0.21]）；策略不匹配和无策略对照组得分分别为0.32和0.21。在此配置下，我们未检测到检索到的子句与金牌子句之间的宏F1差异，尽管置信区间仍然过宽，无法确定非劣效性。第二个检索器和7B模型也出现了相同的定性模式，而在不同微调配置下结果有所变化。这些结果表明，在此基准设置中，精确匹配子句召回率可能低估了下游策略效用，这促使我们在分类循环中使用检索到的策略进行评估，而不仅仅依赖召回率。

Original abstract: Exact-match retrieval recall is often used as a proxy for whether a retriever supplies useful policy context to a downstream decision model. We test this proxy for pre-action policy classification in tau-bench using Qwen2.5-3B/7B classifiers. Under gold-policy conditioning, a compact structured state improves macro-F1 over raw trajectories by 0.13-0.17 after tuning. We then replace the benchmark-designated policy clause with the top-ranked clause retrieved from decision-time context. Although the exact governing clause is retrieved at rank 1 for only 7% of airline states, the primary 3B classifier obtains macro-F1 0.58 with retrieved clauses versus 0.60 with gold clauses (Delta=-0.02, task-cluster 95% CI [-0.23,+0.21]); mismatched-policy and no-policy controls score 0.32 and 0.21. We do not detect a macro-F1 difference between retrieved and gold clauses in this configuration, although the interval remains too wide to establish non-inferiority. The same qualitative pattern appears with a second retriever and at 7B, while varying across fine-tuning configurations. These results indicate that exact-match clause recall can underestimate downstream policy utility in this benchmark setting, motivating evaluation with retrieved policies in the classification loop rather than recall alone.

</details>


### [63] [Towards Spec Learning: Inference-Time Alignment from Preference Pairs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24004v2)
*Dhriti Krishnan,Tejas Goyal,Jaromir Savelka*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出推理时对齐框架spec learning，可用于agent行为控制，但相关性一般。

TL;DR: 提出规范学习框架，通过编译用户指令和偏好判断为自然语言提示来引导LLM，无需参数更新，在密集偏好领域常优于DPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手动构建提示的方法脆弱且易错，偏好微调成本高，需要一种简便低成本的模型引导方法。

Method: 规范学习：利用简短用户指令和少量偏好判断，编译成自然语言规范提示，在推理时条件化LLM，不更新模型参数。

Result: 在偏好信号密集的专业领域数据集上，基于规范生成的响应常优于直接偏好优化（DPO），且规范可读、可解释。

Conclusion: 规范学习提供了一种高效、可解释的替代方案，避免了提示工程和偏好微调的缺点。

中文摘要：将大型语言模型（LLM）引导至期望的行为通常依赖于一个迭代过程，即基于对模型响应的仔细检查来手工制作提示。这是一个复杂、脆弱且容易出错的过程。基于偏好的微调是一种更严谨但通常成本高昂的解决方案。我们提出了规范学习（spec learning）框架，该框架依赖于简短的用户指令和少量的偏好判断。这些被编译成规范，形式为LLM的自然语言提示。规范在推理时对LLM进行条件控制，且无需更新底层模型的参数。我们表明，基于编译规范生成的响应通常在偏好信号密集的专业领域数据集上优于直接偏好优化（DPO）。与不透明的权重更新不同，生成的规范是人类可读的，并且作为产生它们的偏好信号的可解释且透明的书面体现。

Original abstract: Steering a large language model (LLM) toward a desired behavior typically relies on an iterative process of hand-crafting a prompt based on a careful inspection of the model's responses. This is an involved, brittle, and error-prone process. Preference-based fine-tuning is a more rigorous but often prohibitively expensive solution. We propose spec learning, a framework that relies on a brief user instruction and a small set of preference judgments. These are compiled into specifications in the form of natural-language prompts for an LLM. Specifications condition LLMs at inference time, and no parameter updates to the underlying models are required. We show that the responses generated based on the compiled specifications often outperform direct preference optimization (DPO) on datasets from specialized domains whose preference signal is dense. Unlike opaque weight updates, the resulting specifications are human-readable and double as interpretable and transparent written embodiments of the preference signal that produced them.

</details>

### [64] [RoboGaze: Evaluating Robot World Models via Structured Vision-Language Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28385v1)
*Minh-Loi Nguyen,Nghiem Tuong Diep,Hung Khang Nguyen,Minh Le,Doanh Le Thien,Hoang H. Tran,Dung D. Le,Vu N. Duong,Daniel Sonntag,An Thai Le,Duy Minh Ho Nguyen,Vien Anh Ngo,Tran Van Nhiem*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 多agent VLM框架评估机器人世界模型，通用agent评测方法可迁移

TL;DR: RoboGaze是一个无需训练的多智能体VLM框架，用于评估机器人操作生成视频，通过三阶段管道输出结构化故障报告，显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法无法检测生成视频中的物理、时间或逻辑违反，传统指标和单一VLM缺乏泛化性和诊断精度。

Method: RoboGaze采用三阶段流程：任务场景定位、维度特定专家路由和评论者验证，输出基于6维度30类型分类法的时空定位故障报告。

Result: 在382个剪辑数据集上，RoboGaze将描述F1提升43点，时间对齐提升37点，接近人类上限85%；干净剪辑准确率从<25%提升到>80%。

Conclusion: RoboGaze为机器人世界模型评估提供了可扩展、高解释性的诊断工具。

中文摘要：机器人世界模型的最新进展使得用于具身预测和规划的合成视频生成成为可能。然而，评估这些视频具有挑战性：视觉上逼真的输出常常违反物理规律、时间一致性或任务逻辑，而传统指标和单一的视觉语言模型（VLM）裁判无法泛化或提供精确的诊断价值。我们提出RoboGaze，一个无需训练的多智能体VLM框架，为生成的机器人操作视频提供结构化、可解释的评估。给定任务指令和视频，RoboGaze通过三阶段流程运行：任务场景定位、维度特定专家路由以及基于评论者的验证。它输出按照新颖的6维度、30类型机器人特定分类法分类的时间定位故障报告。为了基准测试RoboGaze，我们引入了一个经过人工验证的382个剪辑的数据集，涵盖模拟和真实世界的多视角操作。评估八个开源和专有VLM骨干网络，RoboGaze显著优于零样本基线，将描述F1提升高达+43点，时间对齐（F1 x IoU）提升高达+37点，接近人类上限约85%的差距。此外，其评论者验证器减轻了标准VLM的“狼来了”假阳性缺陷，将干净剪辑准确率从低于25%提升到超过80%。RoboGaze为机器人世界模型的严格评估提供了一个可扩展、高度可解释的诊断工具。

Original abstract: Recent advances in robot world models enable synthetic video generation for embodied prediction and planning. However, evaluating these videos is challenging: visually realistic outputs often violate physical laws, temporal consistency, or task logic, while conventional metrics and monolithic Vision-Language Model (VLM) judges fail to generalize or provide precise diagnostic value. We present RoboGaze, a training-free, multi-agent VLM framework that provides structured, interpretable evaluation for generated robot-manipulation videos. Given a task instruction and video, RoboGaze operates via a three-stage pipeline: task-scene grounding, dimension-specific specialist routing, and critic-based verification. It outputs temporally localized glitch reports categorized under a novel 6-dimension, 30-type robotics-specific taxonomy. To benchmark RoboGaze, we introduce a human-validated dataset of 382 clips spanning simulated and real-world multi-view manipulation. Evaluating eight open-source and proprietary VLM backbones, RoboGaze dramatically outperforms zero-shot baselines, improving description-F1 by up to +43 points and temporal alignment (F1 x IoU) by up to +37 points, closing approximately 85% of the gap to the human ceiling. Furthermore, its critic verifier mitigates the "cry-wolf" false-positive flaw of standard VLMs, lifting clean-clip accuracy from under 25% to over 80%. RoboGaze offers a scalable, highly interpretable diagnostic tool for the rigorous evaluation of robot world models.

</details>


### [65] [AdaReP:Adaptive Re-Planning under Model Mismatch for Neural World-Model Predictive Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23079v1)
*Yutian Cheng,Xiaojian Ma,Xianhao Wang,Min Yang,Rongpeng Su,Hangxin Liu,Xi Chen,Shuai Li,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 自适应重规划方法，可迁移至agent规划模块的容错与效率优化

TL;DR: AdaReP通过在线调整重新规划容忍度，在保持任务性能的同时大幅减少MPC的计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经世界模型与MPC结合时，每一步重新规划计算开销大；重用缓存计划虽能减少开销，但性能依赖于预测失配的传播，需要分析其权衡并改进。

Method: 提出了AdaReP，一种无需训练的包装器，利用当前偏差和局部敏感性在线调整重新规划容忍度。

Result: 在图像空间规划、潜在空间控制和真实机器人操作中，AdaReP显著减少了计算量，任务性能相当，例如物理机器人研究查询减少80%以上。

Conclusion: AdaReP有效地在计算效率和任务性能之间取得平衡，是一种实用的方案。

中文摘要：神经世界模型结合模型预测控制（MPC）在每个环境步骤中重新规划，以限制累积预测误差，但这会带来大量的计算开销。重用缓存的计划可以减少这种开销，但其有效性取决于预测失配在局部动力学中的传播方式。我们通过基于扰动的动态遗憾框架分析了这种权衡，并表明过时计划的惩罚与重用容忍度、自上次重新规划步骤以来的累积失配以及局部动力学的敏感性成正比。基于这一结构，我们提出了AdaReP，这是一种无需训练的包装器，它利用当前与缓存展开的偏差和局部敏感性估计在线调整重新规划容忍度，而不修改学习到的世界模型或规划器。在图像空间规划、潜在空间控制和真实世界机器人操作中，AdaReP显著减少了规划器端的计算量，同时保持了可比较的任务性能，包括在50次试验的物理机器人研究中减少了80%以上的查询。

Original abstract: Neural world models coupled with model predictive control (MPC) replan at every environment step to bound accumulated prediction error, but this incurs substantial computational overhead. Reusing a cached plan reduces this overhead, yet its effectiveness depends on how prediction mismatch propagates through the local dynamics. We analyze this trade-off with a perturbation-based dynamic-regret framework and show that stale-plan penalties scale with the reuse tolerance, the accumulated mismatch since the last replanning step, and the local dynamics sensitivity. Based on this structure, we propose AdaReP, a training-free wrapper that adapts the replanning tolerance online using the current deviation from the cached rollout and a local sensitivity estimate, without modifying the learned world model or planner. Across image-space planning, latent-space control, and real-world robotic manipulation, AdaReP substantially reduces planner-side computation while maintaining comparable task performance, including over 80% fewer queries on a 50-trial physical robot study.

</details>


### [66] [Engineering Reliable Autonomous Systems: Challenges and Solutions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23760v2)
*Marie Farrell,Matt Luckcuck,Angelo Ferrando,Rafael C. Cardoso,Natasha Alechina,Marco Autili,Diana Benjumea Hernandez,Luciana Brasil Rebelo dos Santos,Daniela Briola,Ana Cavalcanti,Christian Colombo,Louise A. Dennis,Clare Dixon,Michael Fisher,Mario Gleirscher,Taylor Johnson,Charles Lesire,Livia Lestingi,Sven Linker,Brian Logan,Colin Paterson,Fabio Papacchini,Patrizio Pelliccione,Pedro Ribeiro,Maike Schwammberger,Silvia Lizeth Tapia Tarifa,Hazel Taylor,Jim Woodcock,Mengwei Xu,Yi Yang,Huan Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 挑战目录及解决方案路径，其中部分挑战有已知学术方法但未实践，其他需进一步研究。

Conclusion: 路线图支持未来研究和工业合作，以解决自主系统工程中的挑战。

中文摘要：工程可靠的自主系统是计算机科学中一个日益重要且不断发展的课题。随着自主系统越来越普及，易于使用的、能够可靠构建它们的技术也变得越来越重要。本研讨会报告捕捉并扩展了2024年6月10日至14日在洛伦兹中心举办的“工程可靠自主系统”（ERAS）研讨会的讨论内容。该研讨会由“自主系统形式化方法研讨会”（FMAS）和“可靠工程化自主性的智能体与机器人研讨会”（AREA）的组织者共同组织，汇聚了FMAS和AREA社区成员、行业从业者以及来自自主系统带来独特工程挑战领域的代表。研讨会聚焦三个主要研究主题：自主系统的验证与确认技术；真实世界自主系统的工程化；以及安全自主系统的软件架构。其主要成果是这些领域中挑战的目录，以及最重要的，通向解决方案的路径。其中一些挑战已经可以通过学术界熟知但尚未在常规实践中使用的技术来解决。其他挑战仍未解决，需要进一步研究。该路线图旨在支持未来的研究和工业合作。

Original abstract: Engineering reliable autonomous systems is an important and growing topic in computer science. As autonomous systems become more prevalent, easy-to-use techniques for building them reliably are increasingly important.
  This workshop report captures and expands on the discussions at the Lorentz Center Workshop "Engineering Reliable Autonomous Systems" (ERAS), held from 10 to 14 June 2024. The workshop was co-organised by the organisers of the Workshop on Formal Methods for Autonomous Systems (FMAS) and the Workshop on Agents and Robots for reliable Engineered Autonomy (AREA). It brought together members of the FMAS and AREA communities, industry practitioners, and representatives from sectors where autonomous systems pose distinctive engineering challenges.
  The workshop focused on three main research topics: techniques for verification and validation of autonomous systems; engineering real-world autonomous systems; and software architectures for safe autonomous systems. Its main outcome is a catalogue of challenges in these areas and, most importantly, a pathway to solutions. Some challenges can already be tackled by techniques that are well known in academia but have not yet become regularly used in practice. Other challenges remain unresolved and require further research. This roadmap is intended to support future research and industrial collaboration.

### [67] [RECALL: Recovery Experience Collection for Active Lifelong Learning in Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23617v1)
*Ulas Berk Karli,Tesca Fitzgerald*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出主动持续学习范式，用于VLA模型，涉及不确定性引导的数据收集与灾难性遗忘缓解，可迁移至agent持续学习。

TL;DR: 提出主动持续学习范式用于VLA模型微调，不确定性引导的数据收集效率更高，但需解决灾难性遗忘问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动模仿学习在VLA微调中存在效率低、浪费演示者精力等问题，需要更主动的数据收集方法。

Method: 采用不确定性引导的主动数据收集进行微调，并结合重放数据混合和弹性权重巩固等技术实现持续学习。

Result: 主动不确定性引导的数据收集比被动收集更高效；但仅用恢复数据微调会导致灾难性遗忘；不同持续学习技术在可塑性与记忆保持间存在权衡。

Conclusion: 不确定性引导的恢复演示能提高适应效率，但将新数据纳入大型策略仍面临开放挑战，需进一步研究平衡可塑性与记忆保持的方法。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通常通过被动模仿学习进行微调，即针对策略表现不佳的任务收集额外的演示数据。这种方法存在几个缺点：需要机器人在触发数据收集之前失败，几乎不提供关于哪些状态需要监督的指导，并且浪费了演示者在策略已经表现良好的冗余任务部分上的努力。在本文中，我们提出了一种主动的、持续学习的VLA范式。我们证明，与使用被动收集的演示相比，主动的、不确定性引导的数据收集能够实现更高效的微调。然而，我们也发现仅对主动收集的恢复数据进行微调会导致灾难性遗忘。我们评估了持续学习的技术，包括基于重放的数据混合和弹性权重巩固，并识别了在针对不确定性引导的恢复数据的可塑性与保留先前学习行为之间的权衡。总的来说，我们的工作为自回归VLA的主动持续学习提供了实证研究，确立了不确定性引导的恢复演示可以提高适应效率，同时揭示了当有针对性的新数据被纳入大型机器人策略时面临的开放挑战。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are commonly fine-tuned through passive imitation learning, where additional demonstrations are collected for tasks where the policy performs poorly. This approach incurs several downsides: it requires the robot to fail before data collection is triggered, provides little guidance about which states require supervision, and wastes demonstrator effort on redundant parts of the task where the policy already performs well. In this paper, we propose an active, continual learning paradigm for VLAs. We demonstrate that active, uncertainty-guided data collection leads to more efficient fine-tuning than when using passively-collected demonstrations. However, we also find that fine-tuning only on actively-collected recovery data leads to catastrophic forgetting. We evaluate techniques for continual learning, including replay-based data mixing and elastic weight consolidation, and identify tradeoffs between plasticity to uncertainty-guided recovery data and retention of previously learned behaviors. Overall, our work contributes an empirical study of active continual learning for autoregressive VLAs, establishing that uncertainty-guided recovery demonstrations can improve adaptation efficiency while also revealing open challenges when targeted new data is incorporated into large robot policies.

</details>

### [68] [What You See Is Not What You Execute: Memory-Based Runtime SBOM Generation for Supply Chain Security](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22827v2)
*Hala Ali,Andrew Case,Irfan Ahmed*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MEM-SBOM是首个直接从Python应用程序运行时状态生成SBOM的内存取证框架，通过恢复模块、解析版本和分析字节码构建依赖图，准确率达100%，优于现有工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SBOM基于元数据或文件系统，无法捕获运行时组件，而运行时检测需提前部署，难以用于生产环境和事件响应。易失性内存可提供无需预设的运行时状态。

Method: MEM-SBOM利用Volatility 3插件，从Python解释器内部结构恢复模块，解析包版本，分析字节码构建依赖图并识别漏洞函数。

Result: 在51个真实应用上达到100%提取准确率，识别出Streamlit调用tornado漏洞，恢复所有现有工具遗漏的运行时包，依赖图和漏洞评估更准确。

Conclusion: MEM-SBOM提供了对系统执行内容的取证合理运行时视图，为软件供应链安全和事件响应提供实用基础。

中文摘要：现代软件开发严重依赖来自公共存储库的第三方组件，扩大了软件供应链攻击面。为应对这些日益增长的风险，联邦计划推动了软件物料清单（SBOM）作为标准化机制，通过描述软件组件、依赖关系及其关系来提高透明度。然而，基于元数据或文件系统工件构建的SBOM无法捕获在运行时加载和执行的组件，尤其是在动态生态系统中，例如Python。此外，通过检测生成运行时SBOM需要提前部署监控，并且系统在整个执行过程中保持可观测性。这些条件在生产环境和事件响应场景中难以满足。相比之下，易失性内存提供了可靠来源，无需事先检测即可恢复运行中应用程序的实际运行时状态。因此，本文提出了MEM-SBOM，这是第一个直接从Python应用程序运行时状态生成SBOM的内存取证框架。它从解释器内部结构中恢复模块，解析包版本，并分析字节码以构建依赖图并识别易受攻击的函数。我们将MEM-SBOM实现为一套Volatility 3插件，并针对51个真实世界的Python应用程序进行了评估。它实现了100%的提取准确率，识别出Streamlit是唯一调用tornado依赖的易受攻击例程的应用程序，并恢复了现有SBOM工具遗漏的所有运行时包，提供了更准确的依赖图和更好的漏洞评估。这些能力通过提供对系统上执行内容的取证合理的运行时视图，使MEM-SBOM成为软件供应链安全和事件响应的实用基础。

Original abstract: Modern software development relies heavily on third-party components from public repositories, expanding the software supply chain attack surface. In response to these growing risks, federal initiatives have advanced the Software Bill of Materials (SBOM) as a standardized mechanism for improving transparency by describing software components, dependencies, and their relationships. However, SBOMs built from metadata or filesystem artifacts fail to capture the components loaded and executed at runtime, especially in dynamic ecosystems such as Python. Moreover, generating runtime SBOMs through instrumentation requires monitoring to be deployed in advance and the system to remain observable throughout execution. Such conditions are difficult to satisfy in production environments and incident-response scenarios. Volatile memory, in contrast, provides a reliable source for recovering the actual runtime state of a running application without requiring prior instrumentation. Therefore, this paper presents MEM-SBOM, the first memory forensics framework that generates SBOMs directly from the runtime state of Python applications. It recovers the modules from the interpreter's internal structures, resolves package versions, and analyzes bytecode to build dependency graphs and identify vulnerable functions. We implemented MEM-SBOM as a suite of Volatility 3 plugins and evaluated it against 51 real-world Python applications. It achieves 100% extraction accuracy, identifies Streamlit as the only application that calls the vulnerable routines of the tornado dependency, and recovers all runtime packages missed by existing SBOM tools, providing more accurate dependency graphs and better vulnerability assessment. These capabilities make MEM-SBOM a practical foundation for software supply chain security and incident response by providing a forensically sound runtime view of what is executed on a system.

</details>


### [69] [Safety in Self-Evolving LLM Agent Systems: Threats, Amplification, and Case Studies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23075v1)
*Ruixiao Lin,Xinhao Deng,Qingming Li,Jianan Ma,Yunhao Feng,Yuqi Qing,Zhenyuan Li,Yechao Zhang,Shiwen Cui,Changhua Meng,Tianwei Zhang,Xingjun Ma,Qi Li,Ke Xu,Shouling Ji*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 自进化LLM agent安全威胁分析，直接相关agent安全控制

TL;DR: 自我演化LLM代理系统将攻击从会话级提升为血统级，静态防御无效，演化原生设计激活更多攻击面且攻击持久率达100%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我演化LLM代理系统引入新威胁，对抗影响被永久编码、自我放大并传播，现有安全分析不足。

Method: 提出模块生命周期攻击面（MLAS）矩阵，分解为5模块×5阶段，分析25个单元格并识别关键威胁和跨领域放大效应。

Result: 17/25单元格面临无缓解的关键威胁；演化原生设计激活3.5倍攻击面，攻击持久率100%，静态防御仅阻止2.5%攻击。

Conclusion: 自我演化使攻击从会话绑定变为血统持久，产生新攻击类，需演化感知安全框架和形式化验证。

中文摘要：自我演化的LLM代理系统能够自主更新其模型参数、记忆、工具和架构，引入了一种全新的威胁格局，其中对抗性影响被永久编码、跨代自我放大，并在没有持续攻击者访问的情况下通过群体传播。我们提出了一种围绕模块生命周期攻击面（MLAS）矩阵的系统性安全与隐私分析，该矩阵将攻击面分解为五个功能模块（大脑、认知资源、执行、自我设计、集体）乘以五个生命周期阶段（引导、提议、评估、提交、服务）。对所得25个单元格的分析表明，其中17个面临关键威胁，且没有有效的部分缓解措施。我们识别出七种跨领域放大效应，它们协同作用，无法通过单独保护各个模块来解决。对两个开源框架的对比案例研究表明，演化原生设计激活的攻击面单元格数量是后者的3.5倍，并实现了100%的攻击持久率（所有CIA+隐私类别的40/40有效载荷），而同地部署的安全扫描器仅阻止了2.5%的攻击。我们的发现表明，自我演化将每个已知攻击类别从会话绑定转变为血统持久，产生了全新的攻击类别，并使静态防御在结构上不足，从而推动了对自我修改系统的演化感知安全框架和形式化验证。

Original abstract: Self-evolving LLM agent systems, which autonomously update their model parameters, memory, tools, and architectures, introduce a qualitatively new threat landscape in which adversarial influences become permanently encoded, self-amplify across generations, and propagate through populations without sustained attacker access. We present a systematic security and privacy analysis organized around the Module-Lifecycle Attack Surface (MLAS) matrix, which decomposes the attack surface into five functional modules (Brain, Cognitive Resource, Execution, Self-Design, Collective) $\times$ five lifecycle stages (Bootstrap, Propose, Evaluate, Commit, Serve). Analysis of the resulting 25 cells reveals that 17 face critical threats for which no effective partial mitigation. We identify seven cross-cutting amplification effects that interact synergistically and cannot be addressed by securing individual modules in isolation. Comparative case studies of two open-source frameworks demonstrate that evolution-native design activates $3.5\times$ more attack surface cells and achieves a 100% attack persistence rate (40/40 payloads across all CIA+Privacy categories), while co-located security scanners block only 2.5% of attacks. Our findings establish that self-evolution converts every known attack category from session-bounded to lineage-persistent, gives rise to entirely new attack classes, and renders static defenses structurally inadequate, motivating evolution-aware security frameworks and formal verification for self-modifying systems.

### [70] [Understanding the (In)Security of Vibe-Coded Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23130v2)
*Junquan Deng,Zhiyu Fan,Ruijie Meng*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了AI代理开发的氛围编码应用程序的安全性，发现其存在独特的漏洞模式（如占位逻辑、未过滤输入、秘密暴露），源于AI的系统性局限，且改进LLM只能降低风险而不能消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氛围编码将大量开发工作委托给AI，引发了对这类应用安全性的根本疑问。

Method: 收集使用流行AI代理开发的真实应用语料库，设计结合代理辅助代码审计和人工验证的漏洞分析框架。

Result: 发现三种主要漏洞模式（占位逻辑、未过滤输入、秘密暴露），归因于AI代理的记忆丢失、局部优化和安全知识不足，且LLM进步可减少但无法消除风险。

Conclusion: 提供了对氛围编码应用安全格局的实证理解，为应对AI委托开发的安全挑战奠定基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展使得“氛围编码”（vibe coding）成为可能，这是一种新兴的软件开发范式，用户主要通过自然语言与AI代理交互来创建应用程序。由于其低门槛，氛围编码在实际应用中迅速普及。与传统的AI辅助编程（开发者仍需负责实现和代码审查）不同，氛围编码将相当大一部分开发工作委托给AI系统。这种转变引发了一个基本问题：通过氛围编码开发的应用程序有多（不）安全？在本文中，我们对氛围编码应用程序的安全性进行了系统研究。我们收集了使用流行AI代理开发的大量真实世界应用程序语料库，并设计了一个结合代理辅助代码审计和人工验证的漏洞分析框架。利用该框架，我们考察了已部署的氛围编码应用程序中漏洞的普遍性、严重性和根本原因。我们的研究揭示了几个关键发现：（1）氛围编码应用程序表现出与常规软件开发工作流中常见漏洞模式不同的重复性漏洞模式，包括占位逻辑、未过滤输入和秘密暴露；（2）这些漏洞源于AI代理在整个氛围编码生命周期中的系统性局限，例如记忆丢失、局部优化目标和安全知识不足；（3）虽然LLM能力的进步和改进的提示策略可以减少漏洞的发生，但它们并不能消除潜在的安全风险。总体而言，我们的研究提供了对氛围编码应用程序安全格局的实证理解，并为基础工作奠定了基础，以应对软件开发日益向AI系统委托所带来的安全挑战。

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have enabled vibe coding, an emerging software development paradigm in which users create applications primarily through natural-language interactions with AI agents. Due to its low barrier to entry, vibe coding is rapidly gaining adoption in practice. Unlike conventional AI-assisted programming, where developers remain responsible for implementation and code review, vibe coding delegates a substantial portion of development to AI systems. This shift raises a fundamental question: how (in)secure are applications developed through vibe coding? In this paper, we conduct a systematic study of the security of vibe-coded applications. We collect a large corpus of real-world applications developed using popular AI agents and design a vulnerability analysis framework that combines agent-assisted code auditing with human validation. Using this framework, we examine the prevalence, severity, and root causes of vulnerabilities in the deployed vibe-coded applications. Our study reveals several key findings: (1) vibe-coded applications exhibit recurring vulnerability patterns that differ from those commonly observed in conventional software development workflows, including placeholder logic, unfiltered input, and secret exposure; (2) these vulnerabilities arise from systematic limitations of AI agents throughout the vibe-coding lifecycle, such as memory loss, locally optimized objectives and insufficient security knowledge; and (3) while advances in LLM capabilities and improved prompting strategies can reduce the incidence of vulnerabilities, they do not eliminate the underlying security risks. Overall, our study provides an empirical understanding of the security landscape of vibe-coded applications and lays the groundwork for addressing the security challenges introduced by the growing delegation of software development to AI systems.

### [71] [Detecting Malicious Agent Skills in the Wild using Attention](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23416v1)
*Bacem Etteib,Daniele Lunghi,Tégawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对恶意agent技能的检测方法，涉及agent安全，但对代码优化agent有间接启发。

TL;DR: 提出Locate-and-Judge两阶段检测器，用于检测LLM代理技能市场中的恶意技能，通过注意力引导的跨度定位和详细判断，实现低成本高精度的大规模检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理技能市场成为新的攻击面，恶意技能可窃取数据或劫持代理，而现有提示注入防御不适用于技能作为指令体的情况。

Method: 两阶段检测器：第一阶段轻量级定位器根据指令跟随注意力对技能结构跨度评分并保留前K个；第二阶段裁判详细检查保留跨度，通过集中判断于高注意力跨度实现可扩展审计。

Result: 与直接LLM扫描相比成本降低一个数量级，召回率略有下降；优于关键词和正则表达式基线；以高精度标记恶意技能，发现数十个真实恶意技能，包括绕过现有检测器的伪装技能。

Conclusion: Locate-and-Judge可有效且低成本地检测技能市场中的恶意技能，具有实际部署价值，并发布了标记数据集。

中文摘要：LLM代理越来越多地加载技能，即由第三方编写并通过市场分发的基于文件的自然语言指令包，这些指令以用户权限执行。单个恶意技能可以窃取数据、劫持代理或作为供应链的立足点持续存在，这使技能市场成为代理系统的新攻击面。提示注入防御无法适用于此场景。它们依赖于可信指令和不可信数据之间的边界，而技能本身是一组指令，因此注入的命令与许多合法命令并存并继承其权限。我们提出了Locate-and-Judge，一种针对该场景设计的两阶段检测器。轻量级的定位器根据每个跨度吸引的指令跟随注意力对技能的结构化跨度进行评分，并仅保留前K个。然后，裁判详细检查保留的跨度。将昂贵的判断集中在少数高注意力跨度上，使检测器能够审计整个市场而不是样本。与直接基于LLM的扫描相比，这种方法提供了数量级的成本降低，在牺牲少量召回率的情况下显著提高了可扩展性，并且在相当的成本下优于关键词和正则表达式基线。以市场规模部署且成本极低，Locate-and-Judge以高精度标记技能，我们手动确认其中大多数为恶意，发现了数十个活跃的恶意技能，包括几个伪装成良性功能的技能，以及许多SkillSpector和Cisco Skill Scanner未能检测到的技能。我们发布了生成的标记数据集。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly load skills, file-based packages of natural-language instructions written by third parties and distributed through marketplaces, that execute with the user's privileges. A single malicious skill can exfiltrate data, hijack the agent, or persist as a supply-chain foothold, which turns the skill marketplace into a new attack surface for agentic systems. Prompt-injection defenses do not carry over to this setting. They rely on a boundary between trusted instructions and untrusted data, whereas a skill is itself a body of instructions, so an injected command sits among many legitimate ones and inherits their authority. We present Locate-and-Judge, a two-stage detector designed for this regime. A lightweight locator scores the structural spans of a skill by the instruction-following attention each span draws and retains only the top-K. A judge then examines the retained spans in detail. Concentrating the costly judgment on a few high-attention spans lets the detector audit an entire marketplace instead of a sample. Compared to direct LLM-based scanning, this approach offers an order-of-magnitude cost reduction, dramatically increasing its scalability at a small cost to recall, and it dominates keyword and regex baselines at comparable expense. Deployed at marketplace scale and at negligible cost, Locate-and-Judge flags skills with high precision, the majority of which we manually confirmed as malicious, surfacing dozens of live malicious skills, including several disguised as benign functionality and many that SkillSpector and Cisco Skill Scanner fail to detect. We release the resulting labeled dataset.

</details>


### [72] [Cryptographic certificates of validity for trustworthy AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23768v1)
*Murdoch J. Gabbay*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出加密证书验证agent行为，涉及agent可信与安全，通用方法。

TL;DR: 提出使用密码学证明系统为AI系统行为提供有效性证书，允许独立验证行为符合策略，无需信任或重计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在形式化验证和密码学认证之间寻求平衡，使智能体行为可被独立验证，无需信任智能体或重新执行计算。

Method: 将策略条件形式化为逻辑谓词，编译为多项式约束的见证检查问题，利用简洁密码学证明系统（如zk-SNARKs）生成可独立验证的证明。

Result: 提出了一个中间方案，智能体行为可附带独立可检查的证明，验证者无需信任智能体或重新执行计算。

Conclusion: 该方案结合了形式化验证和密码学认证的优点，但需进一步解决规范、审计和部署问题。

中文摘要：我们提出针对自主人工智能系统的密码学有效性证书。核心思想是将正确性或策略条件形式化地指定为一个逻辑谓词，将该谓词编译为一个关于多项式约束的见证检查问题，并使用简洁的密码学证明系统（可选地使用零知识）来证明该条件成立。这提供了源代码形式化验证与密码学认证之间的中间地带。智能体的行为可以附带一个独立可验证的证明，证明其满足商定的正式策略，而无需验证者信任该智能体或重新执行计算。我们高层面概述了该方法，给出了核心数学转换，将该提议与证明携带代码、zkVM、形式化方法和智能体治理联系起来，并指出了完整实施必须解决的规范、审计和部署问题。

Original abstract: We propose cryptographic certificates of validity for agentic AI systems. The core idea is to formally specify a correctness or policy condition as a logical predicate, compile this predicate to a witness-checking problem over polynomial constraints, and use a succinct cryptographic proof system (and optionally zero-knowledge) to certify that the condition holds.
  This offers a middle ground between formal verification of source code, and cryptographic authentication. An agent's action can be accompanied by an independently checkable proof that it satisfies an agreed formal policy, without requiring the verifier to trust the agent or to re-execute computation. We outline the approach at a high level, give the core mathematical translation, relate the proposal to proof-carrying code, zkVMs, formal methods, and agent governance, and note the specification, auditing, and deployment questions that a full implementation must answer.

### [73] [Maestro Order: A Model-Agnostic Orchestration Harness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23983v1)
*Hidayet Aksu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出模型无关编排框架，通过分解、集成、验证和递归提升可靠性，是通用agent架构的核心参考。

TL;DR: 提出Maestro Order框架，通过分解、集成、验证和递归四种原语以及预算感知控制器，将不可靠的模型转化为可靠的问题解决系统，并通过蒙特卡洛模拟验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型等强大模型在单次前向传递中快速但不可靠，自信的错误（幻觉）可能导致危险，需要一种系统化的方法来提升其可靠性。

Method: 设计Maestro Order编排框架，包含四个结构原语（分解、集成、验证、递归）和预算感知控制器，将模型视为黑盒求解器，层叠在线测量的验证器集成，动态分配验证和投票资源。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟显示：验证几何级数提升可靠性（如0.55→0.98→0.999），投票仅在高于随机时有效且受限于共享错误，预算感知控制器以极低成本达到目标可靠性。

Conclusion: 构建鲁棒检查器、多样化求解器，并让控制器将计算资源分配给信息最丰富的阶段，同时需注意验证器博弈、相关错误和分解错误累积等失败模式。

中文摘要：一个有能力的模型的单次前向传递是一个快速、流畅但不可靠的问题解决者：它正确得足够频繁以至于有用，错误得足够频繁以至于危险；在语言模型中，这种自信的错误被称为幻觉。我们提出了Maestro Order，一个与模型无关的编排框架，通过根据四个结构原语（分解、集成、验证和递归）以及一个预算感知控制器（决定在哪里花费计算资源）来组合不可靠的求解器，从而将它们转化为可靠的问题解决系统。该框架将任何模型视为统一接口后的黑盒基础求解器，层叠一个判别能力在线测量的验证器集成，并将验证和投票分配给每单位成本边际可靠性最高的阶段。我们给出了架构、消息和状态模式、控制器算法以及使其具有确定性、可观察性和容错性的工程实现。然后我们指定了评估方法（固定成本下的可靠性、覆盖率、校准和消融实验），并报告了在参数化求解器/验证器模型上对该框架进行忠实蒙特卡洛模拟的结果。模拟定量地再现了预测的规律：验证以几何级数放大可靠性（例如，两个门控从0.55到0.98，四个门控到0.999），投票仅在高于随机水平时才有帮助且受限于共享错误，而预算感知控制器通过为每个机制选择最便宜的方法，以投票成本的一小部分达到目标可靠性。最后，我们讨论了失败模式（验证器博弈、相关错误和分解错误累积）并给出了具体指导：构建鲁棒的检查器、多样化求解器，并让控制器将计算放在信息所在之处。

Original abstract: A single forward pass of a capable model is a fast, fluent, and unreliable problem-solver: it is right often enough to be useful and wrong often enough to be dangerous; in language models, such confident errors are known as hallucinations. We present Maestro Order, a model-agnostic orchestration harness that turns unreliable solvers into reliable problem-solving systems by composing them according to four structural primitives (decompose, ensemble, verify, and recurse) and a budget-aware controller that decides where to spend compute. The harness treats any model as a black-box base solver behind a uniform interface, layers a verifier ensemble whose discrimination is measured online, and allocates verification and voting to the stages with the highest marginal reliability per unit cost. We give the architecture, the message and state schema, the controller algorithm, and the engineering that makes it deterministic, observable, and fault-tolerant. We then specify an evaluation methodology (reliability at fixed cost, coverage, calibration, and ablations) and report results from a faithful Monte Carlo simulation of the harness over a parameterized solver/verifier model. The simulation reproduces the predicted laws quantitatively: verification amplifies reliability geometrically (e.g. $0.55\to0.98$ with two gates, $\to0.999$ with four), voting helps only above chance and is limited by shared errors, and a budget-aware controller reaches a target reliability at a small fraction of the cost of voting alone by selecting the cheapest mechanism for each regime. We close with failure modes (verifier gaming, correlated errors, and decomposition error compounding) and concrete guidance: build robust checkers, diversify solvers, and let the controller put compute where the information is.

</details>

### [74] [Discovering Crystal Structure Prediction Algorithms with an AI Co-Scientist](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22866v1)
*Kiyoung Seong,Nayoung Kim,Sungsoo Ahn*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 人机协同系统跨域搜索算法发现，虽在材料科学但方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出人类-AI协同发现系统HACO，通过跨域搜索和稀疏人类引导，从视觉领域迁移MaskGIT并加入晶体学知识，构建了MaskGXT模型，在晶体结构预测任务上取得最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学算法发现依赖领域专家直觉和试错，效率低且难以跨领域迁移。作者希望利用AI自动搜索跨域方法，结合人类稀疏引导，加速科学算法发现。

Method: HACO系统先从跨域搜索识别MaskGIT，将其离散令牌模型适配到晶体结构，再根据人类高层次目标逐步添加对称性令牌、空间群分层采样和子箱坐标细化，形成MaskGXT模型。

Result: MaskGXT在MP-20多晶型划分上METRe准确率达79.06%，高于基线70.87%；在MP-20和MPTS-52标准基准上均取得最佳匹配率。

Conclusion: 在验证廉价、快速且对齐良好的领域，迁移引导的交互式AI协同科学家能通过结合跨域可迁移原理和人类领域指导，有效贡献于科学算法发现。

中文摘要：我们提出了人类-AI协同发现系统（HACO），用于通过跨域搜索和稀疏人类引导实现科学算法发现。从从化学成分生成晶体结构的目标出发，HACO跨多个领域搜索生成建模方法，并识别出MaskGIT（一种来自视觉领域的掩码生成模型）作为晶体结构预测（CSP）的有前景框架。HACO将这种掩码公式实例化为晶体结构的离散令牌模型；在稀疏高层次人类目标的引导下，它随后添加了晶体学对称性令牌、用于多晶型覆盖的空间群分层采样以及子箱坐标细化，从而产生了掩码生成晶体变换器（MaskGXT）。在MP-20多晶型划分上，MaskGXT达到了79.06%的“每个人都匹配到参考”（METRe）准确率，而最强评估基线为70.87%。MaskGXT还在标准MP-20和MPTS-52 CSP基准上取得了最佳匹配率。这些结果证明，在提供廉价、快速且对齐良好的验证的领域中，迁移引导的交互式AI共同科学家可以通过识别可迁移的建模原理并将其与有针对性的人类领域指导相结合，为科学算法发现做出贡献。

Original abstract: We introduce Human-AI Co-discovery system (HACO) for scientific algorithm discovery through cross-domain search and sparse human steering. Starting from the goal of generating crystal structures from chemical compositions, HACO searched across generative modeling methodologies from multiple fields and identified MaskGIT, a masked generative model from vision, as a promising framework for crystal structure prediction (CSP). HACO instantiated this masked formulation as a discrete token model of crystal structure; guided by sparse high-level human objectives, it then added crystallographic symmetry tokens, space group stratified sampling for polymorph coverage, and sub-bin coordinate refinement, yielding the Masked Generative Crystal Transformer (MaskGXT). On the MP-20 polymorph split, MaskGXT reaches 79.06% match-everyone-to-reference (METRe) accuracy, compared with 70.87% for the strongest evaluated baseline. MaskGXT also attains the best match rate on standard MP-20 and MPTS-52 CSP benchmarks. These results provide evidence that, in domains offering cheap, fast, and well-aligned validation, transfer-guided interactive AI co-scientists can contribute to scientific algorithm discovery by identifying transferable modeling principles and combining them with targeted human domain guidance.

### [75] [Provable Benefits of RLVR over SFT for Reasoning Models: Learning to Backtrack Efficiently](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22938v1)
*Stanley Wei,Juno Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 理论分析RLVR为何优于SFT，涉及推理回溯，对agent训练方法有一般性启示。

TL;DR: 理论分析表明，强化学习微调（RLVR）相比监督微调（SFT）在思维链推理中能实现指数级更优的回溯效率，并通过蒸馏传递这一能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释为什么强化微调比监督微调在推理能力上更优，特别是回溯效率的差异。

Method: 将思维链推理建模为图上的路径发现问题，比较RLVR和SFT的理论性能，并证明RLVR能学习高效回溯，而SFT不能。

Result: RLVR方法在推理时计算量上比SFT有指数级优势，并能通过蒸馏传递回溯能力。

Conclusion: RLVR通过仅使用结果奖励教会模型高效回溯，从而更好地分配推理计算资源，且这种能力可被蒸馏。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展表明，对预训练基础模型进行强化微调可以在推理时显著提升推理性能。在这项工作中，我们从理论上分析了为什么强化微调比纯监督微调（SFT）方法能诱导出更好的推理能力。我们将思维链（CoT）推理建模为图上的路径发现问题，并比较了流行的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）方法与传统的SFT。我们证明，SFT在没有负例的情况下训练于黄金最短路径时，无法学习有效回溯。相比之下，RLVR训练的模型能够仅使用结果奖励就学会从死胡同中高效回溯。这导致两种方法在推理时计算量上存在指数级差距，并表明RLVR引导模型学习推理链中困难决策的位置，最终实现推理时计算资源的更好分配。最后，我们展示了RLVR模型的推理轨迹可以被蒸馏，以训练基础模型也高效回溯。

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated that reinforcement fine-tuning of pretrained base models can lead to significant gains in reasoning performance at inference time. In this work, we theoretically analyze why reinforcement fine-tuning induces better reasoning ability than purely supervised fine-tuning (SFT) methods. We model chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning as a pathfinding problem on graphs and compare the popular method of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) against traditional SFT. We prove that SFT, when trained on golden shortest paths without negative examples, fails to learn how to efficiently backtrack. In contrast, an RLVR-trained model can learn how to efficiently backtrack from dead ends using only outcome reward. This leads to an exponential separation in inference-time compute between the two methods, and demonstrates that RLVR leads the model to learn the location of difficult decisions in a reasoning chain, ultimately allowing for better allocation of inference-time compute. Finally, we show that the reasoning traces of an RLVR model can be distilled to train a base model to backtrack efficiently as well.

</details>


### [76] [Attacking the Trusted Imagination: Oracle-Level Integrity Attacks on Imagine-then-Act World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22966v1)
*Linghan Chen,Kaiyan Ji,Minyu Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 攻击想象-行动世界模型，涉及agent安全与鲁棒性，对VLA agent有参考价值。

TL;DR: 发现VLA策略中世界-动作模型的想象易受攻击，破坏了依赖该想象的下游系统（如MPC），但反应性策略保持鲁棒；攻击可被简单检测器在高AUC下识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别VLA策略中信任的想象模块是攻击面，而反应性策略本身并非脆弱点，从而揭示系统鲁棒性依赖于下游组件。

Method: 采用L∞有界观测扰动，通过投影梯度下降攻击完全可微的观测到想象映射；利用离流形属性设计无参数去噪检测器。

Result: 无目标破坏效果强（比随机强60倍），检测AUC=1.0；目标控制受限；自适应攻击者只有放弃破坏才能逃逸；反应性策略鲁棒，但想象驱动MPC首次出现任务失败（成功率从0.70降至0.05）。

Conclusion: VLA系统的鲁棒性评估必须考虑下游预言机对想象输出的依赖；简单的去噪检测器可有效防御无目标攻击，但自适应攻击仍需进一步研究。

中文摘要：许多最近的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略采用“想象-然后行动”的设计。一个世界-动作模型（WAM）首先将短期未来想象为潜在轨迹z~，然后动作基于此进行条件化。我们识别出这种被信任的想象（而非反应性策略）是暴露的攻击面。下游预言机（如安全门、视觉模型预测控制（MPC）规划器或“想象-然后检查”验证器）将z~作为未来预测来使用。因此，策略的鲁棒性并不等同于依赖WAM的系统的鲁棒性。其底层现象是一种不对称性：破坏想象很容易，因为只需将z~从其自然未来流形中移开；而精确操控想象则很难，因为它必须达到一个指定的流形内目标。我们采用基于能力的威胁模型，具有L无穷有界观测扰动。攻击者通过完全可微的观测到想象映射应用投影梯度下降。相同的离流形属性激发了一个无参数去噪检测器。我们评估了三个目标：RynnVLA-002、LingBot-VA和LaDi-WM。无目标破坏比随机破坏强约60倍，并且在AUC为1.0时被检测到。目标控制仍然受限。自适应攻击者只有放弃破坏才能逃避检测。反应性策略对破坏的想象保持鲁棒。然而，一个本机想象驱动的MPC首次表现出特定于对手的任务失败（在epsilon=0.01时，成功率为0.70对比0.05；Fisher p < 10^-4）。

Original abstract: Many recent vision-language-action (VLA) policies adopt an imagine-then-act design. A world-action model (WAM) first imagines a short future as a latent trajectory z~, on which the action is then conditioned. We identify this trusted imagination, rather than the reactive policy, as the exposed attack surface. A downstream oracle, such as a safety gate, a visual model-predictive-control (MPC) planner, or an imagine-then-check verifier, consumes z~ as a prediction of the future. The robustness of the policy therefore does not entail the robustness of systems that rely on the WAM. The underlying phenomenon is an asymmetry. Corrupting the imagination is easy, since it requires only displacing z~ from its natural-future manifold. Steering it precisely is hard, since it must reach a specified on-manifold target. We adopt a capability-based threat model with an L-infinity-bounded observation perturbation. The attacker applies projected gradient descent through the fully differentiable observation-to-imagination map. The same off-manifold property motivates a parameter-free denoiser detector. We evaluate three targets: RynnVLA-002, LingBot-VA, and LaDi-WM. Untargeted corruption is roughly 60x stronger than random and is detected at AUC 1.0. Targeted control remains bounded. An adaptive attacker evades detection only by forgoing corruption. The reactive policy remains robust to corrupted imagination. A native imagination-driven MPC, however, exhibits the first adversary-specific task failure (at epsilon=0.01, success 0.70 versus 0.05; Fisher p < 10^-4).

</details>


### [77] [Group-Graph Policy Optimization for Long-Horizon Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22995v1)
*Yunan Wang,Minghui Song,Zihan Zhang,Shaohan Huang,Haizhen Huang,Furu Wei,Weiwei Deng,Feng Sun,Qi Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出组图策略优化G2PO，用于长程agent RL，处理稀疏奖励，可直接迁移。

TL;DR: G2PO通过将交互轨迹转化为全局状态图，利用组聚合和边中心优势估计改进信用分配，在长程智能体任务中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL框架在长程任务中因奖励稀疏和延迟、忽略状态转换的图结构而导致高方差和局部信用分配，亟需更全局的优化方法。

Method: 提出G2PO，构建全局状态转换图，采用组聚合状态价值估计和边中心优势估计，通过全局标准化TD误差识别关键转换。

Result: 在WebShop、ALFWorld和AppWorld上，G2PO超越基线，相对GRPO成功率提升达22.2%。

Conclusion: G2PO通过图结构化信用分配有效解决长程RL瓶颈，在智能体任务中表现优异。

中文摘要：基于组的强化学习（RL）显著增强了大型语言模型（LLM）在智能体场景中的能力。为了实现更细粒度的策略更新，最近的智能体RL框架已从轨迹级训练转向步骤级训练。然而，长时间跨度的智能体RL面临严重的奖励稀疏性和延迟问题，因为反馈通常延迟数十个交互步骤。虽然现有的步骤级框架细化了训练粒度，但其信用分配仍然是粗粒度的，并且仍然将智能体探索视为孤立的线性轨迹。这种过度简化的视角忽略了状态转换的固有图结构，导致状态价值估计的高方差和短视、局部的信用分配。为了克服这些关键瓶颈，我们提出了组图策略优化（G2PO），这是一种专门为多轮智能体任务设计的新型基于组的RL算法。G2PO明确地将线性交互轨迹转换为全局状态转换图。通过聚合不同轨迹中的相同观测，我们引入了组聚合状态价值估计，以减少采样方差和轨迹依赖偏差。此外，我们将智能体动作重新定义为状态节点之间的转换，并提出了一种以边为中心的优势估计策略。通过在整个图上全局标准化时间差分误差，G2PO明确识别并优先考虑驱动绝对任务进展的关键转换。在代表性的长时间跨度基准（WebShop、ALFWorld和AppWorld）上的大量实验表明，G2PO显著优于最先进的基于提示和RL的基线，相对于GRPO实现了高达22.2%的成功率提升。

Original abstract: Group-based Reinforcement Learning (RL) has significantly enhanced Large Language Models (LLMs) in agentic scenarios. To achieve finer-grained policy updates, recent agentic RL frameworks have shifted from trajectory-level to step-level training. However, long-horizon agentic RL suffers from severe reward sparsity and delay, as feedback is often deferred for dozens of interaction steps. While existing step-level frameworks refine training granularity, their credit assignment remains coarse-grained and still treats agent exploration as isolated, linear trajectories. This oversimplified perspective ignores the inherent graph structure of state transitions, leading to high-variance state-value estimation and myopic, localized credit assignment. To overcome these critical bottlenecks, we propose Group-Graph Policy Optimization (G2PO), a novel group-based RL algorithm tailored for multi-turn agentic tasks. G2PO explicitly transforms linear interaction trajectories into a global state-transition graph. By aggregating identical observations across different trajectories, we introduce group-aggregation state-value estimation that reduces sampling variance and trajectory-dependent bias. Furthermore, we redefine agent actions as transitions between state nodes and propose an edge-centric advantage estimation strategy. By globally standardizing Temporal Difference (TD) errors across the entire graph, G2PO explicitly identifies and prioritizes critical transitions that drive absolute task progress. Extensive experiments on representative long-horizon benchmarks-WebShop, ALFWorld, and AppWorld-demonstrate that G2PO substantially outperforms state-of-the-art prompt-based and RL baselines, achieving remarkable success rate improvements of up to 22.2% over GRPO.

</details>


### [78] [EvoRubrics: Dynamic Rubrics as Rewards via Adversarial Co-Evolution for LLM Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23038v1)
*Hongxin Ding,Baixiang Huang,Yue Fang,Weibin Liao,Zheng Li,Jinyang Zhang,Zhijing Wu,Junfeng Zhao,Yasha Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出对抗性共演化RL框架，策略与奖励生成器联合改进，可迁移至agent自我改进

TL;DR: 提出EvoRubrics，通过策略与量规生成器的协同演化实现实时自适应奖励，避免饱和和破解，提升强化学习性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态量规在训练中逐渐失效，动态方法依赖外部信息且粒度粗，需更优的自适应奖励机制。

Method: 设计协同演化框架，策略LLM和量规生成器在训练步骤中对抗交互，量规生成器根据策略改进动态调整标准，实现实时追踪和自动课程。

Result: EvoRubrics在多个基准上优于静态和动态基线；学到的量规生成器可迁移；完全自监督变体也获得意义增益。

Conclusion: 生成与评估的协同演化能提供足够丰富的学习信号，实现高效、自适应的强化学习。

中文摘要：基于量规的奖励为强化学习提供了可解释且细粒度的优化信号，适用于没有可验证答案的开放任务。然而，预先构建的量规在训练过程中保持静态，与不断演变的策略存在根本性不匹配：固定的标准随着模型改进逐渐丧失判别能力，导致奖励饱和及潜在的奖励破解。最近的动态量规方法部分解决了这个问题，但依赖外部前沿模型或真实答案，且仅以粗粒度更新量规。我们提出EvoRubrics，一种协同演化的强化学习框架，其中策略LLM和量规生成器在每个训练步骤中通过对抗性交互共同改进。随着策略在量规生成器指导下改进，量规生成器调整其标准以保持判别性和信息性，使评估能够实时跟踪策略，并自然产生自动课程。实验表明，EvoRubrics在多个基准上持续优于静态和动态量规基线。学到的量规生成器进一步泛化为可迁移的奖励模型。值得注意的是，即使是没有外部监督的完全自监督变体也实现了有意义的增益，表明生成与评估之间的协同演化本身就能提供足够丰富的学习信号。我们的代码公开在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/EvoRubrics-2155/。

Original abstract: Rubric-based rewards offer interpretable and fine-grained optimization signals for reinforcement learning in open-ended tasks where verifiable answers are unavailable. However, pre-constructed rubrics remain static throughout training, creating a fundamental mismatch with the evolving policy: fixed criteria gradually lose discriminative power as the model improves, leading to reward saturation and potential hacking. Recent dynamic rubric methods partially address this but rely on external frontier models or ground-truth answers, and update rubrics only at coarse granularity. We propose EvoRubrics, a co-evolutionary RL framework where a Policy LLM and a Rubric Generator jointly improve through adversarial interaction within each training step. As the policy improves under the rubric generator's guidance, the rubric generator adapts its criteria to remain discriminative and informative, enabling evaluation to track the policy in real time and naturally inducing an automatic curriculum. Experiments show that EvoRubrics consistently outperforms static and dynamic rubric baselines across benchmarks. The learned Rubric Generator further generalizes as a transferable reward model. Notably, even a fully self-supervised variant without any external supervision achieves meaningful gains, suggesting that co-evolution between generation and evaluation alone can provide sufficiently rich learning signals. Our code is publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/EvoRubrics-2155/.

</details>


### [79] [ReNIO: Reweighting Negative Trajectory Importance for LLM On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23104v1)
*Chen Lin,Kedi Chen,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 重加权负轨迹的LLM自蒸馏，改进推理能力，可迁移至agent训练

TL;DR: ReNIO通过重新加权负面轨迹的重要性，提升了LLM在线策略蒸馏的性能，在数学推理和代码生成任务上取得了显著增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准在线策略蒸馏平等对待所有学生生成输出，但实验发现错误输出比正确输出更具信息量，因此需要一种无需最终答案即可利用错误信号的方法。

Method: 提出ReNIO，利用学生到教师概率比识别导致错误推理轨迹的关键令牌，聚合为归一化样本权重，自动赋予负面轨迹更高权重，且仅需前缀条件概率。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成任务上，ReNIO提升了OPD和OPSD，Qwen3-1.7B相对增益8.90%，R1-Distill-Qwen-7B相对增益10.00%。

Conclusion: ReNIO有效利用错误输出中的探索性信号，提升了推理能力，并保留了前缀训练优势。

中文摘要：在线策略蒸馏（OPD）通过训练学生模型在其自身生成的输出上，提升了LLM的推理能力，但标准OPD平等对待所有学生生成的输出（SGO），无论其信息量如何。我们在受控过滤实验中观察到一个一致的对称性：在OPD和在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）中，仅在错误SGO上训练优于仅在正确SGO上训练。我们的进一步分析表明，仅在正确SGO上训练的模型倾向于生成更短的推理轨迹，并表现出较弱的反思行为，而错误SGO更好地保留了接近模型能力边界的探索性推理。为了利用这一信号而不需要完整的包含答案的展开，我们引入了ReNIO，它重新加权负面轨迹重要性用于LLM在线策略蒸馏。通过使用学生到教师的概率比，ReNIO识别出导致错误推理轨迹的关键令牌，并将其信息聚合为归一化的样本权重，内在分配给可能的负面轨迹更大的权重，而无需观察最终答案的正确性。由于ReNIO仅使用前缀条件下的令牌概率，它保留了OPD相对于完整展开强化学习的前缀训练优势。在数学推理和代码生成任务中，ReNIO均提升了OPD和OPSD，在数学推理基准上对Qwen3-1.7B和R1-Distill-Qwen-7B分别取得了高达8.90%和10.00%的代表性相对增益。代码仓库：https://github.com/BDML-lab/ReNIO。

Original abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) improves LLM reasoning by training a student model on its own generated outputs, but standard OPD treats all student-generated outputs (SGOs) equally regardless of their informativeness. We observe a consistent asymmetry in controlled filtering experiments: in both OPD and on-policy self distillation (OPSD), training only on incorrect SGOs outperforms training only on correct ones. Our further analysis suggests that models trained on correct-only SGOs tend to generate shorter reasoning traces and show weaker reflection behavior, while incorrect SGOs better preserve exploratory reasoning near the model's capability boundary. To exploit this signal without requiring full answer-containing rollouts, we introduce ReNIO, which Reweights Negative trajectory Importance for LLM On-policy distillation. By using the student-to-teacher probability ratio, ReNIO identifies pivotal tokens leading to wrong reasoning traces and aggregates their information into a normalized sample weight, inherently assigning larger weights to likely negative trajectories without observing the correctness of final-answer. Since Re-NIO only uses prefix-conditioned token probabilities, it preserves OPD's prefix training advantage over full-rollout reinforcement learning. Across both mathematical reasoning and code generation tasks, ReNIO improves both OPD and OPSD, with representative relative gains of up to 8.90% for Qwen3-1.7B and 10.00% for R1-Distill-Qwen-7B on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Code repo: https://github.com/BDML-lab/ReNIO.

</details>


### [80] [Self-Evolution for Multi-Turn Tool-Calling Agents via Divergence-Point Preference Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23112v1)
*Jiaqiang Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多轮工具调用agent通过分歧点偏好学习实现自我进化，直接研究agent训练和工具选择。

TL;DR: 提出ToolGraph结合图结构和DPO偏好学习，在工具使用代理中实现了显著的奖励提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将推理时编排与参数级学习分离，导致工具选择结构弱，且偏好更新易受提示不匹配影响。

Method: 构建ToolGraph，结合模式拓扑、成功轨迹权重和历史感知控制；通过状态匹配和前缀对齐构建偏好对，并用DPO在同一上下文中训练。

Result: 在375个任务上，ToolGraph提升奖励11.2%，ToolGraph+DPO提升16.8%，增益集中在航空和零售领域。

Conclusion: ToolGraph和DPO的结合有效提升了多轮工具使用代理的性能，且特定领域效果显著。

中文摘要：多轮工具使用代理必须协调长程工具序列，同时跟踪对话状态和策略约束。现有方法通常将推理时编排与参数级学习分开，导致工具选择结构弱，偏好更新容易受到训练-部署提示不匹配的影响。为了在基准内自我改进，ToolGraph结合了从模式派生的拓扑、从成功轨迹估计的转换权重以及用于写入先决条件和重复搜索循环的历史感知控制。然后，我们通过基于状态匹配和基于前缀的对齐来定位分歧点，构建了161个偏好对，这些对通过动作正确性注释进行过滤，并在推理时使用的相同ToolGraph上下文中训练DPO。在375个tau2-bench任务中，ToolGraph将加权平均奖励从0.304提升到0.338（相对提升11.2%），而ToolGraph+DPO达到0.355（比基线提升16.8%），其中DPO的增益集中在航空和零售领域。细粒度诊断进一步表明，大约一半的电信轨迹在执行动作之前耗尽了步骤预算，并且在我们评估的16个DPO配置中，选择奖励积极性是最有用的检查点信号。

Original abstract: Multi-turn tool-using agents must coordinate long-horizon tool sequences while tracking dialogue state and policy constraints. Existing approaches often separate inference-time orchestration from parameter-level learning, leaving tool selection weakly structured and preference updates vulnerable to train--deployment prompt mismatch. For within-benchmark self-improvement, ToolGraph combines schema-derived topology, transition weights estimated from successful rollouts, and history-aware controls for write prerequisites and repeated-search loops. We then construct 161 preference pairs by locating divergence points via state-based matching and prefix-based alignment, filtered through action-correctness annotations, and train DPO under the same ToolGraph context used at inference. Across 375 tau2-bench tasks, ToolGraph raises the weighted average reward from 0.304 to 0.338 (+11.2% relative), while ToolGraph+DPO reaches 0.355 (+16.8% over the baseline), with the DPO gain concentrated in airline and retail. Fine-grained diagnostics further show that roughly half of telecom trajectories exhaust the step budget before action execution and that chosen reward positivity is the most useful checkpoint signal across our 16 evaluated DPO configurations.

### [81] [Memory Contagion: Cross-Temporal Propagation of Evaluator Bias via Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23195v2)
*Zewen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 分析agent记忆系统中的偏差传播，对记忆设计和安全性有启发。

TL;DR: 我们发现记忆传染现象：评估者偏见可通过代理记忆跨时间传播，长度偏见可传播而权威偏见不能，且依赖模型代际。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究假设记忆源于无偏见经验，但实际中代理可能受有偏见评估者影响，导致偏见跨时间传播，亟需识别并形式化此现象。

Method: 通过长度偏好和权威偏见两种偏见类型，在四个实验阶段中测试多个模型（DeepSeek V4-Chat等）的记忆传染，使用Gamma_A等指标量化传播。

Result: 长度偏见在旧模型上传播（Gamma_A=13.18），新模型免疫；权威偏见在所有15个实验中未传播（Gamma_A=0.00）；污染率低至0.2时仍可检测到长度偏见传播。

Conclusion: 当前代理记忆设计存在脆弱性，偏见可跨时间传播且无安全阈值，需开发形式化工具进行测量和防御。

中文摘要：大型语言模型(LLM)代理越来越依赖记忆系统来维持长期连贯性。最近的研究表明，在持续整合过程中，代理记忆会退化。然而，现有研究假设记忆源于无偏见的经验。在这项工作中，我们识别并正式定义了一个新现象：记忆传染——评估者偏见通过代理记忆的跨时间传播。我们表明，当代理由有偏见的评估者训练或引导时，他们的经验会变得有偏见；当这些轨迹被存储并整合到记忆中时，偏见会传播给从同一记忆存储中检索的未来代理，即使整合是完美的（oracle）。在两种偏见类型（长度偏好、权威偏见）和四个实验阶段中，我们证明：(1) 即使在较旧模型（Gamma_A = 13.18, DeepSeek V4-Chat）上完美整合，长度偏见也会发生记忆传染，而较新模型（V4-Pro, Claude）则免疫，证明了偏见输入是充分原因，且传染依赖于模型代际；(2) 在所有15个受控多种子实验中，权威偏见未能传播（Gamma_A = 0.00），揭示了并非所有评估者偏见都能通过当前记忆架构跨越时间边界；(3) 未观察到安全阈值：在污染率低至p=0.2时检测到长度偏见传播。我们的发现揭示了当前代理记忆设计中一个关键但偶然的脆弱性，并提供了测量跨时间偏见传播的形式化工具。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents increasingly rely on memory systems to maintain long-term coherence. Recent work shows that agent memories degrade during continuous consolidation. However, existing research assumes memories are derived from unbiased experiences. In this work, we identify and formalize a novel phenomenon: Memory Contagion -- the cross-temporal propagation of evaluator bias through agent memory. We show that when agents are trained or guided by biased evaluators, their experiences become biased; when these trajectories are stored and consolidated into memory, the bias propagates to future agents retrieving from the same memory store, even when consolidation is perfect (oracle). Across two bias types (length preference, authority bias) and four experimental phases, we demonstrate: (1) Memory Contagion occurs for length bias even with perfect consolidation on older models (Gamma_A = 13.18, DeepSeek V4-Chat), while newer models (V4-Pro, Claude) are immune, proving both that biased input is a sufficient cause and that contagion is model-generation-dependent; (2) authority bias fails to propagate in all 15 controlled multi-seed experiments (Gamma_A = 0.00), revealing that not all evaluator biases can cross temporal boundaries through current memory architectures; (3) No observed safe threshold: length bias propagation is detected at contamination rates as low as p=0.2. Our findings expose a critical but contingent vulnerability in current agent memory designs and provide formal tools for measuring cross-temporal bias propagation.

</details>


### [82] [Scheduling Thoughts: Learning the Order of Thought in Diffusion Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23567v1)
*Jiawei Xu,Minghui Liu,Aakriti Agrawal,Yifan Chen,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 扩散语言模型的解码顺序优化，使用GRPO学习策略，类似agent规划，可启发agent中的决策优化。

TL;DR: 提出自感知调度（SAS），将掩码扩散模型的解码顺序选择转化为策略优化问题，通过GRPO学习轻量级顺序策略，在数独和数学推理任务上显著提升生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 掩码扩散模型的解码顺序强烈影响生成质量，但现有方法通常采用启发式选择，缺乏理论指导和优化原则。

Method: 推导了基于路径对数似然的KL散度上界，诱导出自知奖励，将有序轨迹上的顺序选择建模为策略优化问题，并使用GRPO学习轻量级顺序策略，适用于任意顺序和半自回归解码。

Result: 在1B MDM数独任务上，准确率从82.0%提升至97.5%；在LLaDA-8B的GSM8K上pass@1从64%提升至76%，MBPP上从39.5%提升至41%，一致超越启发式调度。

Conclusion: SAS能有效学习最优解码顺序，显著提升生成质量，且可灵活应用于不同任务和模型规模，优于启发式方法。

中文摘要：掩码扩散语言模型通过迭代式地取消掩码来解码，其中取消掩码的顺序定义了一种“思想顺序”，它强烈影响生成质量，但通常是通过启发式选择的。我们推导了一个关于顺序解码失配的可处理上界，该失配用Kullback-Leibler散度度量，并以模型的路径对数似然表示，且在模型充分表达时紧致。这个界在有序轨迹上诱导出一个密集的自知奖励，将顺序选择视为一个原则性的策略优化问题，且去噪器固定。我们将此想法实例化为自感知调度（SAS），它使用Group Relative Policy Optimization学习一个轻量级顺序策略，并无缝地适用于任意顺序和半自回归解码。在包含1B参数MDM的数独任务上，SAS将谜题准确率从82.0%（最佳启发式调度）提高到91.8%，并通过沿学习到的轨迹进行第二阶段微调达到97.5%。在数学推理任务上，使用LLaDA-8B，SAS在GSM8K上将pass@1从64%提高到76%，在MBPP上从39.5%提高到41%，在不同的生成长度和块大小上一致地匹配或超越启发式调度。项目页面：https://jimmyxu123.github.io/SAS

Original abstract: Masked diffusion language models decode by iteratively unmasking tokens, where the unmasking order defines an "order of thought" that strongly influences generation quality yet is typically chosen heuristically. We derive a tractable upper bound on the sequential decoding mismatch, measured by the Kullback-Leibler divergence and expressed in terms of the model's pathwise log-likelihood, with tightness under sufficient model expressivity. This bound induces a dense self-aware reward over ordered trajectories, casting order selection as a principled policy optimization problem with a frozen denoiser. We instantiate this idea as Self-Aware Scheduling (SAS), which learns a lightweight order policy using Group Relative Policy Optimization and applies seamlessly to both any-order and semi-autoregressive decoding. On Sudoku with 1B MDM, SAS improves puzzle accuracy from 82.0% (best heuristic schedule) to 91.8%, and reaches 97.5% with second-stage fine-tuning along learned trajectories. On mathematical reasoning with LLaDA-8B, SAS improves pass@1 on GSM8K from 64% to 76% and on MBPP from 39.5% to 41%, consistently matching or exceeding heuristic schedules across generation lengths and block sizes. Project page: https://jimmyxu123.github.io/SAS

</details>


### [83] [Learning Process Rewards via Success Visitation Matching for Efficient RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23640v1)
*Raymond Tsao,Andrew Wagenmaker,Sergey Levine*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 通过成功访问匹配将稀疏奖励转化为密集过程奖励，适用于agent训练中的奖励塑形，具有通用性。

TL;DR: 提出一种通过判别器将稀疏奖励转化为密集过程奖励的方法，在不改变最优策略的情况下加速强化学习，在机器人操作任务中验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏奖励导致信用分配困难，强化学习收敛慢或无效，需要更密集的反馈信号。

Method: 训练判别器区分成功与失败轨迹，用其输出作为奖励信号，激励策略匹配成功轨迹的状态-动作分布。

Result: 在模拟和真实机器人操作任务中，相比稀疏奖励基线，强化学习微调速度显著加快。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效将稀疏奖励转化为密集过程奖励，提升学习效率且不改变最优策略。

中文摘要：在许多现代强化学习应用中，感兴趣任务的天然奖励本质上是稀疏的：除了任务完成时获得+1奖励外，其他所有情况都获得0奖励。训练策略最大化这种稀疏奖励需要解决具有挑战性的信用分配问题，导致强化学习改进缓慢或无效。我们提出了一种简单的方法，将稀疏的结果奖励转换为密集的过程奖励。我们的方法依赖于训练一个判别器来区分先前成功和未成功的回合，并使用该判别器激励强化学习策略匹配成功回合的状态-动作访问，同时避免未成功回合的访问。通过激励策略匹配所有状态（不仅是那些对应于任务成功的状态）的访问，这种奖励提供了关于是否正在朝着任务完成取得进展的密集反馈，并且我们证明这可以在不改变最优策略的情况下实现。聚焦于机器人控制策略的微调，我们展示了在模拟和真实世界的操作任务中，与简单地最大化稀疏结果奖励相比，我们的方法显著提高了强化学习微调性能。

Original abstract: In many modern applications of reinforcement learning (RL), the natural reward for a task of interest is inherently sparse: a reward of 0 is given everywhere except when the task is completed, when a reward of +1 is given. Training a policy to maximize such a sparse reward requires solving a challenging credit assignment problem, leading to slow or ineffective RL improvement. We propose a simple approach to transform a sparse outcome reward into a dense process reward. Our approach relies on training a discriminator to distinguish between previous successful and unsuccessful episodes, and using this discriminator to incentivize the RL-learned policy to match the state-action visitations of successful episodes, while avoiding those of unsuccessful episodes. By incentivizing the policy to match the visitations over all states, not just those that correspond to task success, this reward provides dense feedback on whether progress is being made towards task completion, and, we show, provably achieves this without changing the optimal policy. Focusing on finetuning of robotic control policies, we demonstrate that our approach leads to significantly faster RL finetuning performance on both simulated and real-world manipulation tasks, as compared to simply maximizing the sparse outcome reward.

</details>

### [84] [LLM-Aided A* Search in Non-Geometric Network Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23136v1)
*Nouf Alabbasi,Esraa Ghourab,Omar Alhussein*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: LLM辅助A*搜索生成中间路径点，可迁移到agent规划中的子目标指引。

TL;DR: 提出LLM辅助A*算法，通过地标距离引导LLM生成中间路点，在非几何图上减少约50%的扩展节点数，路径成本仅微增。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非几何网络图中缺乏几何距离作为启发式，导致A*等知情搜索算法效率低下。

Method: 利用地标距离作为可容许的ALT启发式，并将其作为紧凑结构特征输入LLM，生成中间路点引导A*扩展。

Result: 在多达2000个节点的多个图拓扑上，扩展节点数减少约50%，路径成本边际增加。

Conclusion: 结合LLM生成的路点与经典A*搜索可高效优化非几何网络，且紧凑结构特征比高级提示更有效。

中文摘要：在非几何网络图中寻找最短路径，其中边权重编码任意度量（如延迟或货币成本）而非空间距离，对知情搜索算法构成挑战。其效率取决于信息丰富的启发式，通常在空间域由几何距离提供，但在非几何图中没有对应物。我们提出了一种大语言模型辅助的A*算法，其中LLM生成中间路点，引导A*扩展朝向有希望的图区域。该方法的核心是地标距离，它既作为可容许的基于地标的ALT启发式用于搜索，又作为紧凑的结构特征，提供给LLM以恢复它在非几何图上本会缺失的距离到目的地信号。我们在多达2000个节点的多个图拓扑上的全面实验表明，与最优解相比，LLM生成的路点将扩展节点数减少了约50%，同时仅带来边际路径成本增加。我们进一步分析了提示工程的影响，并表明包含紧凑结构特征（即启发式估计）比高级提示技术更有效。这些发现展示了将基于LLM的指导与经典搜索算法相结合用于高效网络优化的潜力。

Original abstract: Finding the shortest path in non-geometric network graphs, where edge weights encode arbitrary metrics such as latency or monetary cost rather than spatial distance, poses a challenge for informed search algorithms. Their efficiency depends on an informative heuristic, typically supplied in spatial domains by geometric distances that have no counterpart on non-geometric graphs. We propose a large language model (LLM)-aided A* algorithm in which an LLM generates intermediate waypoints that guide the A* expansion toward promising graph regions. At the core of the approach are landmark distances, which serve both as an admissible landmark-based (ALT) heuristic for the search and as a compact structural feature that, supplied to the LLM, restores the distance-to-destination signal it would otherwise lack on non-geometric graphs. Our comprehensive experiments on multiple graph topologies with up to 2,000 nodes demonstrate that LLM-generated waypoints reduce the number of expanded nodes by around 50% while incurring only a marginal path cost increase compared to the optimal solution. We further analyze the impact of prompt engineering and show that incorporating compact structural features, namely heuristic estimates, is more effective than advanced prompting techniques. These findings demonstrate the potential of combining LLM- based guidance with classical search algorithms for efficient network optimization.

</details>


<div id='cs.DC'></div>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [85] [Kamera: Unified Position-Invariant Multimodal KV Cache for Training-Free Reuse](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23581v1)
*Bole Ma,Jan Eitzinger,Harald Koestler,Gerhard Wellein*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 多模态agent的KV缓存重用，训练免费，提升效率，直接相关agent优化。

TL;DR: 提出一种无需训练的低秩条件补丁，通过位置无关块缓存和精确RoPE重旋转，避免多模态代理重复编码，在跨块绑定任务上恢复完整准确率且大幅降低KV占用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存在多模态代理重复检查相同内容时导致不必要的重计算，且朴素KV重用丢失跨块条件，使多跳推理准确率减半。

Method: 为每个位置无关的块存储一个小型低秩条件补丁，结合精确RoPE重旋转操作，实现跨MLA、GQA和MHA的简单重用，支持重排序、滑动窗口生存和召回。

Result: 秩为m的补丁在MM-NIAH和两页文档QA基准上恢复完整任务准确率，KV占用大幅降低，并在生产SGLang内核中重建KV到bf16精度。

Conclusion: 该方法有效消除了多模态代理中的冗余编码，尤其在视觉和视频流中效果显著，是影响最大的解决方案。

中文摘要：多模态代理反复重新检查相同的视频帧、UI截图和渲染的人工制品，随着其上下文窗口滑动和推理迭代，但每次回顾都从头开始重新编码，因为前缀缓存仅在固定的前导位置提供重用。我们展示这种重计算是可以避免的，并确切指出朴素KV重用丢失了什么：一个块从其邻居吸收的跨块条件。这种损失是不对称的。缓存块的直接读出通过标准状态合并被精确且免费地恢复。剩下的是一个集中在深层、低秩的弥散残差，单跳检索不可见，但正是多跳推理所依赖的。因此，盲目重用使单跳召回保持完整，但将多跳准确率减半；这是先前位置无关缓存（设计用于单上下文或单图像重用）未解决的失败模式。我们通过一个小的、无需训练的低秩条件补丁来修复它，该补丁与每个位置无关的块一起存储。重用简化为跨MLA、GQA和MHA的一个操作：精确的RoPE重新旋转到任何目标位置，加上恢复跨块绑定的补丁。这使得三种窗口操作变得廉价：重排序（一个补丁服务于缓存集的任何排序）、滑动窗口存活（存活的块仅通过旋转重新定位，零重新编码）和召回（被驱逐的块通过其补丁重新激活，从不重新编码）。一个秩为m的补丁在跨块绑定基准测试（MM-NIAH跨越两个注意力家族和两页文档QA）上以KV占用的一小部分恢复了完整任务准确率，并在生产SGLang内核中跨六个骨干重建了重填充KV到bf16舍入。条件信号在冗余视觉和视频流中最强，使得我们的解决方案在多模态代理花费其重计算预算的地方影响最大。

Original abstract: Multimodal agents repeatedly re-examine the same video frames, UI screenshots, and rendered artifacts as their context window slides and reasoning iterates, yet every look-back re-encodes from scratch, because prefix caches serve reuse only at a fixed leading position. We show this recompute is avoidable, and identify exactly what naive KV reuse loses: the cross-chunk conditioning a chunk absorbs from its neighbours. This loss is asymmetric. The direct readout of a cached chunk is recovered exactly and for free by the standard state-merge. What remains is a diffuse, low-rank residue concentrated in deep layers, invisible to single-hop retrieval but precisely what multi-hop reasoning binds on. Blind reuse therefore leaves single-hop recall intact while halving multi-hop accuracy; this is the failure mode prior position-independent caches, designed for single-context or single-image reuse, do not address. We repair it with a small, training-free low-rank conditioning patch stored alongside each position-free chunk. Reuse reduces to one operator across MLA, GQA, and MHA: exact RoPE re-rotation to any target position, plus the patch that restores cross-chunk binding. This makes three window operations cheap: reorder (one patch serves every ordering of a cached set), sliding-window survival (surviving chunks relocate via rotation only, zero re-encode), and recall (an evicted chunk is rehydrated by its patch, never re-encoded). A rank-m patch recovers full task accuracy on cross-chunk-binding benchmarks, MM-NIAH across two attention families and two-page doc-QA, at a fraction of the KV footprint, and reconstructs re-prefill KV to within bf16 rounding in a production SGLang kernel across six backbones. The conditioning signal is strongest in redundant vision and video streams, making our solution most impactful where multimodal agents spend their recompute budget.

</details>
