# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [86] [A Set-Theoretic Approach to Detecting Logic Bugs in DBMS Inner Join Optimizations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23294v2)
*Ce Lyu,Changzheng Wei,Yanhao Wang,Jie Liang,Li Lin,Hanghang Wu,Minghao Zhao,Ying Yan,Aoying Zhou*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于集合论的蜕变测试方法JoinEquiv，通过三种语义保持变换规则生成等价查询，系统检测INNER JOIN优化中的逻辑错误，在主流DBMS中发现29个新问题，其中27个已确认。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模糊测试工具主要发现崩溃和性能错误，难以检测逻辑错误（查询结果不正确），而连接优化中的逻辑错误常见且难以检测，需要新的方法。

Method: 基于集合论，利用三种语义保持的变换规则（对称连接变换、非对称差变换、对称差变换）将简单NATURAL/INNER JOIN查询重写为等价复杂形式，通过比较原始与变换后查询结果检测逻辑不一致性，实现为JoinEquiv工具。

Result: 在MySQL、TiDB、DuckDB和Percona中检测到29个新问题，其中27个被官方确认，揭示了优化器和执行器中的深层逻辑缺陷。

Conclusion: JoinEquiv能有效发现DBMS中与连接优化相关的逻辑错误，增强系统稳健性，验证了基于集合论的蜕变测试方法的有效性。

中文摘要：查询优化器是数据库管理系统的基本组件，它通过评估备选查询计划来确定给定查询的最有效执行策略。其中，连接优化扮演着核心角色，因为多表查询中连接的顺序会显著影响执行性能。然而，由于连接优化的固有复杂性，逻辑错误不可避免且难以检测。尽管现有的模糊测试工具在发现崩溃和性能相关错误方面取得了显著成功，但有效识别逻辑错误——系统产生不正确查询结果的情况——仍然在很大程度上未解决。在本文中，我们提出了一种基于集合论的蜕变测试方法，用于检测与INNER JOIN优化相关的DBMS错误。对于每个测试用例，基于基本的集合操作——交集——生成等价查询，并引入了三种语义保持的变换规则，即对称连接变换、非对称差变换和对称差变换。这些规则将一个简单的NATURAL/INNER JOIN查询重写为更复杂但语义等价的形式。我们将此设计实现为JoinEquiv，它作为一个测试预言，通过比较原始查询和变换后查询的结果，系统地揭示DBMS查询处理中的逻辑不一致性。使用JoinEquiv，我们在主流DBMS（MySQL、TiDB、DuckDB和Percona）中发现了29个以前未知的问题，其中27个已得到官方确认。JoinEquiv揭示了DBMS优化器和执行器中的深层逻辑缺陷，突显了其在增强DBMS稳健性方面的价值。

Original abstract: The query optimizer is a fundamental component of database management systems that determines the most efficient execution strategy for a given query by evaluating alternative query plans. Among its tasks, join optimization plays a central role, as the order of joins in multi-table queries can significantly affect execution performance. However, due to the inherent complexity of join optimization, logical bugs are inevitable and often difficult to detect. While existing fuzzing tools have shown notable success in uncovering crash- and performance-related errors, effectively identifying logical bugs -- cases in which the system produces incorrect query results -- remains largely unresolved.
  In this paper, we propose a metamorphic testing approach to detect DBMS bugs related to INNER JOIN optimization through the lens of set theory. For each testing case, equivalent queries are generated based on a basic set operation -- intersection -- and three semantics-preserving transformation rules, i.e., symmetric join transformation, asymmetric difference transformation, and symmetric difference transformation, are introduced. These rules rewrite a simple NATURAL/INNER JOIN query into a more complex, yet semantically equivalent, form. We implement this design in JoinEquiv, which serves as a testing oracle to systematically uncover logical inconsistencies in DBMS query processing by comparing the results of original and transformed queries. Using JoinEquiv, we uncovered 29 previously unknown issues in mainstream DBMSs (MySQL, TiDB, DuckDB, and Percona), and 27 of them were officially confirmed. JoinEquiv reveals deep logical flaws in DBMS optimizers and executors, underscoring its value in enhancing DBMS robustness.

</details>


### [87] [SQLConductor: Search-to-Policy Learning for Step-wise Text-to-SQL Orchestration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23537v1)
*Yizhang Zhu,Zhangyang Peng,Boyan Li,Yuyu Luo*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: Text-to-SQL步骤式编排学习，使用MCTS和强化学习学习规划策略，可迁移到coding agent的工作流组合。

TL;DR: 提出SQLConductor，一种逐步编排学习框架，通过策略模型动态选择动作，结合搜索到策略学习和课程强化学习，在Text-to-SQL任务上取得SOTA结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Text-to-SQL系统要么采用固定流水线缺乏自适应性，要么采用先规划后执行的方法无法利用中间反馈，需要一种能根据中间结果动态调整工作流的灵活方法。

Method: SQLConductor将子任务建模为动作，训练策略模型逐步选择动作；使用蒙特卡洛树搜索探索工作流，通过稳定性估计提取高质量监督，经稳定加权微调和课程强化学习训练策略。

Result: 在BIRD-Dev上达到73.2%执行准确率，优于直接训练更大骨干网络的方法，并在分布外数据集上表现良好。

Conclusion: SQLConductor通过逐步编排有效适应不同查询需求，实现了强泛化和高准确率，验证了动态工作流组合的优越性。

中文摘要：Text-to-SQL使用户能够通过自然语言访问关系数据库，但现实环境由于需要对复杂数据库环境进行协调推理而仍然具有挑战性。现有系统通常采用多阶段流水线或针对单个阶段专门化的推理模型。然而，固定的流水线依赖于预定义的阶段顺序，限制了其对查询需求和中间证据的自适应性。最近基于编排的方法通过为每个查询组合专门的模块提供了灵活性，但典型的先规划后执行的方法仍然在执行前承诺一个完整的工作流，无法适应中间结果和反馈。在本文中，我们提出了SQLConductor，一种用于Text-to-SQL的逐步编排学习框架。SQLConductor将Text-to-SQL子任务形式化为用于工作流组合的专门动作，并训练一个策略模型根据中间结果和反馈选择下一个动作。为了学习该策略，SQLConductor引入了搜索到策略学习（Search-to-Policy Learning），该方法使用蒙特卡洛树搜索来探索候选工作流，并使用稳定性估计来识别鲁棒的监督信号。策略模型通过稳定性加权监督微调（Stability-weighted Supervised Fine-tuning）进行训练，以优先考虑高质量的编排模式，并通过课程强化学习（Curriculum Reinforcement Learning）进一步增强。这将离线工作流搜索转化为推理时用于逐步编排的可部署策略。在BIRD-Dev和分布外数据集上的实验表明，SQLConductor实现了优越的执行准确率和强大的泛化能力，在BIRD-Dev上使用紧凑的编排策略协调冻结的更大动作模型达到了73.2%的执行准确率，优于直接训练相当或更大Text-to-SQL骨干网络的先前方法。进一步分析表明，所学策略能够使编排适应多样化的查询需求。

Original abstract: Text-to-SQL enables users to access relational databases via natural language, but real-world settings remain challenging due to coordinated reasoning over complex database environments. Existing systems often use multi-stage pipelines or reasoning models specialized for individual stages. However, fixed pipelines rely on predefined stage orders, limiting their adaptivity to query demands and intermediate evidence. Recent orchestration-based methods provide flexibility by composing specialized modules for each query, but typical plan-then-execute approaches still commit to a complete workflow before execution and cannot adapt to intermediate artifacts and feedback.
  In this paper, we propose SQLConductor, a step-wise orchestration learning framework for Text-to-SQL. SQLConductor formulates Text-to-SQL subtasks as specialized actions for workflow composition and trains a policy model to select the next action based on intermediate artifacts and feedback. To learn this policy, SQLConductor introduces Search-to-Policy Learning, which uses Monte Carlo Tree Search to explore candidate workflows and stability estimation to identify robust supervision. The policy model is trained with Stability-weighted Supervised Fine-tuning to prioritize high-quality orchestration patterns and further enhanced through Curriculum Reinforcement Learning. This transforms offline workflow search into a deployable policy for step-wise orchestration at inference time. Experiments on BIRD-Dev and out-of-distribution datasets show that SQLConductor achieves superior execution accuracy and strong generalization, reaching 73.2% EX on BIRD-Dev with a compact orchestration policy coordinating frozen larger action models, outperforming prior methods that directly train comparable or larger Text-to-SQL backbones. Further analyses show that the learned policy adapts orchestration to diverse query demands.

</details>

### [88] [ESBMC-PLC+: A Unified IEC 61131-3 Formal Verification Framework as a PLCverif Successor](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23870v2)
*Pierre Dantas,Lucas Cordeiro,Waldir Junior*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ESBMC-PLC+ 是首个通过单一 ESBMC 后端支持 IEC 61131-3 三种主要输入格式（LD、ST、图形化 LD）的开源 PLC 验证框架，实现了无界安全证明，并在定时器程序上比 nuXmv BDD 快数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 PLC 验证平台 PLCverif 不支持梯形图（LD）且依赖有界证明的 CBMC 后端，而先前针对 ESBMC 的工作未覆盖结构化文本（ST）和带定时器/计数器的图形化 LD，因此需要统一框架填补这些空白。

Method: 通过 MATIEC 编译器实现 ST/SCL 前端，将 C 编译后的 ST 与 ESBMC 结合，并引入非确定性输入建模和 YAML 属性注入；同时为图形化 LD 扩展 DFS 解析器，将定时器、计数器和边沿触发器建模为 GOTO IR 中的持久状态变量。

Result: ESBMC-PLC+ 匹配 PLCverif 的输入覆盖范围，支持所有三种 IEC 61131-3 格式；在 8 个基准程序上，相比 nuXmv BDD 后端，定时器程序快 400-2000 倍，且在 nuXmv 超时的情况下完成证明。

Conclusion: ESBMC-PLC+ 是首个开源的统一 PLC 验证框架，通过单一后端同时支持 LD、ST 和图形化 LD，并实现 k-归纳无界安全证明，为工业 PLC 验证提供了更强的保证和性能优势。

中文摘要：PLCverif 是 CERN 开发的最成熟的开源 PLC 形式验证平台，自 2019 年起投入生产使用。但它有两个根本性限制：不支持梯形图（LD）程序（PLC 的主要表示法），以及依赖 CBMC 作为主要后端，这限制了验证仅限于有界证明。PLCverif 的作者自己将 ESBMC 确定为适当的后端改进。先前的工作建立了 ESBMC-PLC（一个带有 k-归纳的文本 LD 前端）和 ESBMC-GraphPLC（图形化 PLCopen XML 支持）；两者共同覆盖了 LD 的无界证明，但不支持结构化文本（ST），并且带有定时器/计数器功能块的图形化 LD 仍然无法验证。本文提出 ESBMC-PLC+，一个统一的框架，填补了这两个空白：（1）通过 MATIEC IEC 61131-3 编译器实现的 ST/SCL 前端，将 C 编译后的 ST 路由到 ESBMC，并配有非确定性输入建模和 YAML 属性注入；（2）图形化 LD 的功能块状态语义，扩展了 DFS 解析器，将 TON/TOF/TP 定时器、CTU/CTD 计数器以及 R_TRIG/F_TRIG 边沿触发器建模为 GOTO IR 中持久的扫描周期状态变量。ESBMC-PLC+ 是首个通过单一 ESBMC 后端支持所有三种主要 IEC 61131-3 输入格式的开源 PLC 验证框架，支持 k-归纳无界安全证明。与 PLCverif 的功能对比以及在 8 个基准程序（包括多达 8 个整数定时器的程序）上的实验评估表明，ESBMC-PLC+ 在匹配 PLCverif 输入覆盖范围的同时提供了更强的保证。相比于 nuXmv 的 BDD 后端，ESBMC-PLC+ 在定时器程序上快 400-2000 倍，并在 nuXmv BDD 在 120 秒超时的情况下完成证明。

Original abstract: PLCverif is the most mature open-source platform for PLC formal verification, developed at CERN and in production use since 2019. Yet it has two fundamental limitations: no support for Ladder Diagram (LD) programs, the dominant PLC notation, and reliance on CBMC as its primary backend, which restricts verification to bounded proofs. The PLCverif authors themselves identified ESBMC as the appropriate backend improvement. Prior work established ESBMC-PLC (a textual LD frontend with k-induction) and ESBMC-GraphPLC (graphical PLCopen XML support); together, they cover LD with unbounded proofs but not Structured Text (ST), and graphical LD with timer/counter function blocks remains unverifiable. This paper presents ESBMC-PLC+, a unified framework that closes both gaps: (1) an ST/SCL frontend via the MATIEC IEC 61131-3 compiler, routing C-compiled ST to ESBMC with nondeterministic input modeling and YAML property injection; (2) function block state semantics for graphical LD, extending the DFS resolver to model TON/TOF/TP timers, CTU/CTD counters, and R_TRIG/F_TRIG edge triggers as persistent scan-cycle state variables in the GOTO IR. ESBMC-PLC+ is the first open-source PLC verification framework to support all three major IEC 61131-3 input formats via a single ESBMC backend, enabling k-induction-unbounded safety proofs. A feature comparison with PLCverif and experimental evaluation on 8 benchmark programs, including programs with up to 8 integer timers, shows that ESBMC-PLC+ matches PLCverif's input coverage while providing stronger guarantees. Against nuXmv's BDD backend, ESBMC-PLC+ is 400-2,000x faster on timer programs and completes proofs where nuXmv BDD times out at 120s.

</details>

### [89] [VeriPilot: An LLM-Powered Verilog Debugging Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23759v1)
*Yihan Wang,Cheng Liu,Jiazheng Zhang,Lei Zhang,Long Cheng,Xiaowei Li,Huawei Li*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: VeriPilot是一个利用黄金参考模型和LLM进行Verilog调试的框架，通过内部变量对齐和CDFG追踪实现精准定位和修复，在CVDP基准上将GPT-4o修复成功率从54.3%提升至85.71%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM调试方法仅依赖输出和编译器反馈，难以处理复杂错误，尤其是长依赖链和大代码库中的问题。

Method: 提出VeriPilot框架，利用黄金参考模型进行内部变量语义对齐，通过CDFG进行逐步信号追踪，识别最小可疑代码区域并指导LLM修复。

Result: 在CVDP基准上，VeriPilot将GPT-4o的修复成功率从54.3%提高到85.71%。

Conclusion: VeriPilot显著提升了复杂Verilog设计的错误定位和修复效果，并开源了代码和基准。

中文摘要：Verilog调试仍然是数字电路设计中最耗时的阶段之一。大型语言模型（LLM）的最新进展实现了自动调试；然而，大多数现有方法仅以端到端方式依赖测试输出和编译器反馈，限制了其在复杂错误上的有效性。一个关键挑战是，错误的根本原因可能远离其可观察的输出，使得LLM难以追踪代码中的长依赖链。这一挑战在大型代码库中进一步加剧，因为长上下文长度阻碍了高效推理。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了VeriPilot，一个基于LLM的调试框架，利用黄金参考模型实现细粒度的错误定位和修复。VeriPilot超越了输出级比较，通过基于LLM的分析对齐Verilog设计与其对应黄金模型之间的内部变量语义。然后，它使用从静态分析中导出的控制数据流图（CDFG）进行逐步信号追踪，识别出最小可疑代码区域及其来自黄金模型的正确对应部分。这些结构化见解随后提供给LLM以指导推理和自动代码修复。在NVIDIA的综合Verilog设计问题（CVDP）基准上的实验结果表明，VeriPilot将GPT-4o的修复成功率从54.3%提高到85.71%，显著提升了复杂Verilog设计的错误定位精度和修复效果。源代码和基准可在Github https://github.com/YihanWn/VeriPilot.git上公开获取。

Original abstract: Verilog debugging remains one of the most time-consuming stages in digital circuit design. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled automated debugging; however, most existing approaches rely solely on test outputs and compiler feedback in an end-to-end manner, limiting their effectiveness on complex bugs. A key challenge is that the root cause of an error may be far removed from its observable outputs, making it difficult for LLMs to trace long dependency chains in code. This challenge is further exacerbated in large codebases, where long context lengths hinder efficient reasoning. To address these limitations, we propose VeriPilot, an LLM-powered debugging framework that leverages golden reference models to enable fine-grained bug localization and repair. VeriPilot goes beyond output-level comparison by aligning internal variable semantics between the Verilog design and its corresponding golden model through LLM-based analysis. It then performs step-by-step signal tracing using Control-Data-Flow Graphs (CDFGs) derived from static analysis, identifying a minimal set of suspicious code regions along with their correct counterparts from the golden model. These structured insights are subsequently provided to the LLM to guide reasoning and automated code repair. Experimental results on the Comprehensive Verilog Design Problems (CVDP) benchmark from NVIDIA demonstrate that VeriPilot improves the repair success rate of GPT-4o from 54.3\% to 85.71\%, significantly enhancing both bug localization accuracy and repair effectiveness for complex Verilog designs. The source code and benchmark are publicly available at Github https://github.com/YihanWn/VeriPilot.git.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [90] [Intend, Reflect, Refine: An Adaptive Multimodal Reflection Framework for Autonomous Driving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22913v1)
*Zisheng Chen,Yuping Qiu,Jianhua Han,Tao Tang,Xiuwei Chen,Likui Zhang,Ying-Cong Chen,Hang Xu,Xiaodan Liang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 自动驾驶中的自适应多模态反思框架，反思机制可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出IRR-Drive自适应多模态反思框架，通过预测未来BEV和文本意图进行自我修正，实现场景复杂度驱动的轨迹规划，在NAVSIM上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型直接生成最终轨迹而不评估未来后果，在复杂动态环境中可靠性不足。

Method: IRR-Drive先生成文本意图并预测未来语义BEV，构建双模态反思空间进行自我修正；设计自适应反思奖励，使模型根据场景复杂度选择推理模式，并将反思机制集成到规划框架中。

Result: 在NAVSIM基准的PDMS和EPDMS指标上均取得最先进性能。

Conclusion: 多模态反思框架和自适应反思策略在自动驾驶规划中有效，能提升可靠性和性能。

中文摘要：最近，视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通过引入推理能力，提升了端到端自动驾驶的可解释性和规划质量。然而，现有大多数方法直接生成最终轨迹，没有明确检查其未来后果，这限制了它们在复杂动态环境中的可靠性。为了解决这一限制，我们提出了IRR-Drive（意图、反思、细化），一种用于自动驾驶的自适应多模态反思框架。具体而言，为了将高层推理与物理约束紧密耦合，IRR-Drive首先生成初步的文本意图，并通过预测未来语义鸟瞰图（BEV）表示来预见潜在的交互。这种双模态（文本+BEV）反思空间显式地建模了预期的场景演变，使模型能够在生成最终轨迹之前严格自我纠正并细化其初始意图。此外，为了平衡规划性能和计算效率，我们构建了面向反思的训练数据，并设计了自适应反思奖励，使模型能够根据场景复杂度自适应地选择推理模式。IRR-Drive并非将推理主要用作辅助解释，而是直接将自适应反思机制集成到规划框架中，实现了由场景复杂度驱动的基于实际、决策感知的轨迹修正。我们的方法在NAVSIM基准测试的PDMS和EPDMS指标上均达到了最先进水平。大量实验证明了我们多模态反思框架的有效性，并验证了所提出的自适应反思策略的效能。

Original abstract: Recent Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have advanced end-to-end autonomous driving by incorporating reasoning for better interpretability and planning quality. However, most existing approaches directly generate the final trajectory without explicitly examining its future consequences, which limits their reliability in complex and dynamic environments. To address this limitation, we propose IRR-Drive (Intend, Reflect, Refine), an adaptive multimodal reflection framework for autonomous driving. Specifically, to tightly couple high-level reasoning with physical constraints, IRR-Drive first generates a preliminary textual intention and anticipates potential interactions by predicting future semantic bird's-eye view (BEV) representations. This dual-modality (Text + BEV) reflection space explicitly models anticipated scene evolution, enabling the model to rigorously self-correct and refine its initial intent before generating the final trajectory. Furthermore, to balance planning performance and computational efficiency, we construct reflection-oriented training data and design an adaptive reflection reward, enabling the model to adaptively select its reasoning mode according to scene complexity. Instead of using reasoning primarily as an auxiliary interpretation, IRR-Drive directly integrates an adaptive reflection mechanism into the planning framework, enabling grounded, decision-aware trajectory correction that is driven by scene complexity. Our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on the NAVSIM benchmark in both PDMS and EPDMS. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our multimodal reflection framework and validate the efficacy of the proposed adaptive reflection strategy.

</details>


### [91] [RS-Gen: A Multi-Stage Agentic Framework for Reasoning and Search-Augmented Image Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23221v1)
*Feifei Bian,Zhimin Zheng,Wei Deng,Daiguo Zhou,Jian Luan*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多阶段agent框架用于图像生成，包含推理和搜索增强，可迁移到一般agent。

TL;DR: 提出RS-Gen，一个即插即用、无需训练的多阶段图像智能体框架，通过“提问-解决”闭环机制增强逻辑推理和知识填补，在WISE Verified和RISEBench上分别提升0.313和19.70，达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像模型在处理模糊意图、逻辑推理和OOD知识时，由于缺乏深度推理和实时外部信息而表现次优；统一模型受限于参数规模和静态知识缺口。

Method: RS-Gen是一个即插即用、无需训练的多阶段图像智能体框架，引入“提问-解决”闭环机制，自动识别逻辑问题和知识缺口，并自主规划行动以弥补信息缺失和进行深度逻辑推理。

Result: 在WISE Verified和RISEBench基准上，RS-Gen使Qwen-Image提升0.313，Qwen-Image-Edit-2511提升19.70，均达到开源模型SOTA水平。

Conclusion: RS-Gen显著扩展了基础图像生成和编辑模型的能力边界，成功将模型提升至最先进水平。

中文摘要：近年来，图像生成和编辑领域取得了显著进展，特别是在指令遵循和视觉保真度方面。然而，在处理模糊意图、逻辑推理和分布外（OOD）知识时，现有图像模型由于缺乏深度推理能力和实时外部信息，往往产生次优结果。尽管新兴的统一理解与生成模型试图弥补这一差距，但它们仍受限于自身的参数规模和静态知识缺口。受智能体范式的启发，我们提出了RS-Gen：一个即插即用、无需训练的多阶段图像智能体框架。RS-Gen创新性地引入了“提问-解决”闭环机制，以准确识别逻辑问题和知识缺口，自主规划行动以弥补信息缺失并执行深度逻辑推理。大量实验表明，RS-Gen显著扩展了基础图像生成和编辑模型的能力边界。具体来说，在WISE Verified和RISEBench基准上，RS-Gen分别为Qwen-Image和Qwen-Image-Edit-2511带来了0.313和19.70的绝对性能提升，成功将两者提升至开源模型中的最先进（SOTA）水平。

Original abstract: Recent years have witnessed remarkable progress in image generation and editing, particularly regarding instruction following and visual fidelity. However, when handling ambiguous intentions, logical reasoning, and Out-of-Distribution (OOD) knowledge, existing image models often yield sub-optimal results due to a lack of deep reasoning capabilities and real-time external information. Although emerging unified understanding-and-generation models attempt to bridge this gap, they remain constrained by their intrinsic parameter scales and static knowledge gaps. Inspired by agentic paradigms, we propose RS-Gen: a plug-and-play, training-free, multi-stage image agentic framework. RS-Gen innovatively introduces a "Questioning-and-Solving" closed-loop mechanism to accurately identify logical issues and knowledge gaps, autonomously planning actions to bridge information deficits and execute deep logical reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RS-Gen significantly expands the capability boundaries of foundational image generation and editing models. Specifically, on the WISE Verified and RISEBench benchmarks, RS-Gen yields substantial absolute performance gains of 0.313 for Qwen-Image and 19.70 for Qwen-Image-Edit-2511, respectively, successfully elevating both to the state-of-the-art (SOTA) level among open-source models.

</details>


### [92] [VideoAgent: All-in-One Framework for Video Understanding and Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23327v2)
*Hengji Zhou,Lingxuan Huang,Jian Wang,Bing Zhou,Si Wu,Lianghao Xia,Chao Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 视频编辑多agent框架，包含意图解析、工具编排与多agent协作，架构可迁移至其他agent系统。

TL;DR: 提出VideoAgent，一个通过自动镜头创建和多智能体编排实现长视频理解与编辑的通用框架，在性能和成本上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频编辑自动化系统只能处理短片段和特定任务，无法进行多样化操作和长视频连贯叙事。

Method: 通过自动视频镜头创建（含镜头规划智能体和跨模态检索）以及多智能体编排框架（含30多个专门编辑智能体、意图解析和文本梯度图优化）实现。

Result: 在VideoEdit基准上实现87-95%编排成功率，API成本降低60%，人工评估仅比人类创作低4%。

Conclusion: VideoAgent是首个全能的视频编辑智能体框架，显著优于现有大模型和智能体系统，生成专业质量内容。

中文摘要：视频编辑已成为数字媒体创作中不可或缺的一部分，然而现有的自动化系统局限于短片段处理和特定领域的任务。它们面临两个关键限制：i) 无法处理多样化的视频理解和编辑操作，以及ii) 缺乏长视频理解以实现连贯的叙事创作。我们提出VideoAgent，一个全能的智能体框架，通过两个关键创新来解决这些挑战。首先，我们开发了自动化视频镜头创建，包括用于连贯叙事的镜头规划智能体和用于对齐视觉内容的跨模态检索。其次，我们设计了一个多智能体编排框架，集成了三十多个专门的编辑智能体。意图解析筛选相关工具，而文本梯度图优化组装复杂的编辑流水线。在我们新提出的VideoEdit基准和公开数据集上的大量实验表明，VideoAgent优于现有的多模态大语言模型和智能体系统。VideoAgent实现了87-95%的编排成功率，同时将API成本降低了60%。跨六个视频类别的人工评估显示，VideoAgent生成的专业质量内容接近人类水平，评分仅比人工创建的视频低4%。我们在https://github.com/HKUDS/VideoAgent上发布代码。

Original abstract: Video editing has become essential in digital media creation, yet existing automated systems are restricted to short segment processing and domain-specific tasks. They face two critical limitations: i) inability to handle diverse video comprehension and editing operations, and ii) lack of long-video understanding for coherent narrative creation. We propose VideoAgent, an all-in-one agentic framework addressing these challenges through two key innovations. First, we develop automated video shot creation with shot planning agents for coherent narratives and cross-modal retrieval for aligned visual content. Second, we design a multi-agent orchestration framework integrating over thirty specialized editing agents. Intent parsing filters relevant tools while textual-gradient graph optimization assembles complex editing pipelines. Extensive experiments on our newly-proposed VideoEdit benchmark and public datasets demonstrate VideoAgent's superiority over existing multimodal LLMs and agentic systems. VideoAgent achieves 87-95% orchestration success rates while reducing API costs by 60%. Human evaluation across six video categories shows VideoAgent produces professional-quality content approaching human-level performance, with ratings only 4% below human-created videos. We release our code at https://github.com/HKUDS/VideoAgent.

</details>


### [93] [AwakeForest: An Interactive Geospatial Platform for Large-Scale Forest Imagery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23542v1)
*Suraj Prasai,Kangning Cui,Rongkun Zhu,Sarra Alqahtani,Ying Zhang,Victor Paul Pauca,Miles R. Silman,Fan Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AwakeForest是一个集模型辅助推理、自动标注和人在回路精炼于一体的交互式端到端平台，专为大规模森林图像分析设计，支持可扩展的云优化工作流和即插即用模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具缺乏一个统一、地理空间原生、云优化且机器学习集成的平台，无法处理森林图像分析中端到端工作流的规模和复杂性。

Method: 提出AwakeForest平台，集成模型辅助推理、自动标注和人在回路精炼，支持预训练模型即插即用和可扩展的图像交互。

Result: 在PALMS数据集上验证，AwakeForest支持端到端工作流，生成分析就绪输出，并支持迭代更新。

Conclusion: AwakeForest提供了一个实用的工具，用于大规模森林图像分析，能够简化工作流并支持实际森林管理。

中文摘要：森林图像分析通常涉及多个紧密耦合的视觉任务，这些任务必须在地理区域、传感器和采集条件的显著变化下执行。然而，从业者通常缺乏一个统一工具，该工具应具有地理空间原生、云优化和机器学习集成特性，以支持从标注、预测、可视化到大规模下游分析的端到端工作流。我们提出了AwakeForest，一个专为大规模森林图像设计的交互式端到端平台，它在单个工作流中集成了模型辅助推理、自动标注和人在回路精炼。我们的平台支持预训练模型的即插即用集成，并能够实现与森林图像的可扩展交互，这些图像范围从标准航拍场景到可能跨越数GB到数百GB的大型正射影像马赛克。AwakeForest生成可直接用于下游分析的分析就绪输出，并支持在新场景上进行迭代模型和标注更新。我们在PALMS数据集上展示了该系统，并说明了AwakeForest如何支持用于实际森林管理和分析的端到端工作流。

Original abstract: Forest imagery analysis often involves multiple tightly coupled vision tasks, which must be performed under substantial variation in geographic regions, sensors, and acquisition conditions. However, practitioners often lack a unified tool that is geospatial-native, cloud-optimized, and ML-integrated for end-to-end workflows spanning annotation, prediction, visualization, and downstream analysis at scale. We present AwakeForest, an interactive end-to-end platform designed for large-scale forest imagery that integrates model-assisted inference, automatic annotation, and human-in-the-loop refinement within a single workflow. Our platform supports plug-and-play integration of pretrained models and enables scalable interaction with forest imagery ranging from standard aerial scenes to large orthomosaics that can span several gigabytes to hundreds of gigabytes. AwakeForest produces analysis-ready outputs that can be directly used for downstream analysis and to support iterative model and annotation updates on new scenes. We demonstrate the system on the PALMS dataset and illustrate how AwakeForest supports an end-to-end workflow for practical forest management and analysis.

</details>


### [94] [AIR: Adaptive Interleaved Reasoning with Code in MLLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23678v1)
*Cong Han,Xiaohan Lan,Haibo Qiu,Yujie Zhong*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出自适应代码交织推理与工具调用的强化学习框架，直接面向coding agent

TL;DR: 通过强化学习和代码增强，使多模态大模型在数值计算任务上实现自适应交错推理，性能提升6.1个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖预定义启发式规则，无法处理数值计算问题。

Method: 提出三组件方案：两阶段冷启动数据构建、RL数据过滤、基于组约束奖励函数的自适应工具调用策略。

Result: 评估基准性能平均提升6.1pp，交错推理准确率提升9.9pp，工具使用成功率超95%。

Conclusion: 强化学习训练代码增强的推理有效提升多模态大模型在复杂数值计算任务上的能力。

中文摘要：遵循OpenAI o3开启的范式转变，使用代码交错推理来增强多模态大模型（MLLMs）已成为关键研究前沿。现有文献主要关注视觉感知任务中的工具使用。然而，这类方法通常依赖预定义的视觉操作启发式规则，且由于仅关注视觉操作，本质上无法解决数值计算问题。本文通过扩展强化学习训练在代码增强的复杂数值计算任务上，赋予MLLMs自适应交错推理能力。为此，我们提出了一个包含三个组件的综合解决方案：两阶段冷启动数据构建流水线、用于RL数据集筛选的数据过滤策略，以及利用组约束奖励函数进行交错推理轨迹的自适应工具调用策略。大量实验表明，在采用组约束奖励函数进行强化学习训练后，在评估基准上性能平均提升了6.1个百分点（pp）。具体而言，交错推理样本的准确率提升了9.9 pp，工具使用的总体成功率超过95%。我们的数据和代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/CongHan0808/AIR.git。

Original abstract: Following the paradigm shift initiated by OpenAI o3, interleaved reasoning with code to enhance multimodal large language models (MLLMs) has become a pivotal research frontier. The existing literature focuses primarily on tool-use within vision-perception tasks. However, such approaches typically rely on predefined heuristics for visual manipulation and are inherently incapable of addressing numerical computation problems due to their exclusive focus on visual operations. This paper empowers MLLMs with adaptive interleaved reasoning capabilities through extended reinforcement learning training on code-augmented complex numerical computation tasks. To this end, we propose a comprehensive three-component solution consisting of: a two-stage cold-start data construction pipeline, data filtering strategies for RL dataset curation, and an adaptive tool-invocation strategy leveraging a group-constrained reward function for interleaved reasoning trajectories. Extensive experiments demonstrate that after Reinforcement Learning training with the group-constrained reward function, performance improves by an average of 6.1 percentage points (pp) on evaluation benchmarks. Specifically, the accuracy for interleaved reasoning samples increases by 9.9 pp, and the overall success rate of tool-use exceeds 95%. Our data and code are available at: https://github.com/CongHan0808/AIR.git.

</details>

### [95] [Composition: Building Community with Arts, Math, and Code (Experience Report)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23526v1)
*Isidore Mohr,Claire Wang*

Main category: cs.MM

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文报告了Composition活动系列的组织经验，包括活动结构、艺术家选拔、推广策略及社区反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分享跨学科活动组织的实践经验，以促进艺术、数学与代码领域的交流。

Method: 通过描述活动结构、艺术家选择流程、征稿与宣传外联工作，以及收集社区反馈来呈现经验。

Result: 社区反响积极，活动成功举办。

Conclusion: Composition活动系列为艺术、数学与代码的交叉领域提供了有效的交流平台，其组织模式可供类似活动参考。

中文摘要：Composition (https://composition.codes) 是一个关于艺术、数学和代码的免费活动系列。本经验报告涵盖了Composition的活动结构、艺术家选择过程、征稿和活动推广的外联工作，以及社区反响。
